What Are Stereotype Annotations? 
Stereotype annotations in Spring are meta-annotations used to mark a class as a Spring-managed component (bean). These 
annotations automatically register the class into the Spring container, eliminating the need to declare the bean explicitly in 
XML. 
Type of Stereotype Annotations:- 
Annotation Purpose   Scope     Layer It Belongs To   
@Component Generic Spring bean To configure java class as 
Spring bean (bean will be 
created and it is managed by 
IOC container) 
Any layer 
@Service Marks a service class @Component + also makes 
the service class by giving 
Transaction management 
support(Sprign AOP) 
Service layer (Business 
logic) 
@Repository Marks a DAO class @Component + also makes 
the DAO class by Exception 
propogation 
facilities(SQLException to 
Spring specific Exception) 
Persistence layer (DAO) 
`@Controller Marks a web controller @Component + also makes 
the Controller class getting 
the facility of handling 
HttpRequests. 
Presentation layer (Spring 
MVC) 
Note: 
To make IOC container going to different specified packages and their subpackages to search and recognize steroannotations 
classes as SpringBean we need to place  
<context:component-scan package =""/> in xml file. 
These stereo-annotations should be applied only at the class level. 
@Scope annotation: - The @Scope annotation in Spring is used to define how long a bean should live — 
in other words, its lifecycle and visibility within the application.By default, Spring beans are Singleton (only 
one instance per Spring container). But with @Scope, you can change this behavior. 
@Component 
@Scope("prototype") 
package com.Spring.StereoAnnotations; 
public interface Courier { 
 public String deliver(int oid); 
} 
package com.Spring.StereoAnnotations; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Scope; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
@Component(value="bDart") 
@Scope(scopeName = "prototype") 
public class BlueDart implements Courier { 
 static{ 
  System.out.println("BlueDart class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public BlueDart() 
 { 
  System.out.println("BlueDart object is instantiated..."); 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String deliver(int oid) { 
  System.out.println("BlueDart is Delivered.....!"); 
  return "BlueDart Courier will deliver with Order Id :: "+oid+" Order Product"; 
 } 
} 
package com.Spring.StereoAnnotations;

public class DTDC implements Courier {

 @Override

 }

package com.Spring.StereoAnnotationsTarget; 
import java.util.Arrays; 
import java.util.Random; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Qualifier; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Scope; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.Spring.StereoAnnotations.Courier; 
@Component(value="fpkt") 
@Scope(scopeName = "prototype") 
public class Flipkart { 
 //Feild level Autowireing ... 
 @Autowired 
 @Qualifier("dtdc") 
 private Courier courier; 
 private Long regNo; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("Flipkart.class file is loading..."); 
 } 
 public Flipkart() 
 { 
  System.out.println("Flipkart object is created..."); 
 } 
 //@Autowired 
 public Flipkart(@Qualifier("bDart") Courier courier,@Value("256") Long regNo) { 
  System.out.println("FlipKart :: Two Param Constructor...!"); 
  this.courier = courier; 
  this.regNo = regNo; 
 } 
 //@Autowired 
 public Flipkart(@Qualifier("fFlight") Courier courier) { 
  System.out.println("Flipkart object is created through Constructor:: One param constructor"); 
  this.courier = courier; 
 } 
// @Autowired 
 public void setCourier(@Qualifier("dtdc") Courier courier) { 
  System.out.println("Courier object is injected through Setter"); 
  this.courier = courier; 
 } 
 public void setRegNo(Long regNo) { 
  this.regNo = regNo; 
 } 
 public long getRegNo() 
 { 
  return regNo; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "Flipkart [courier=" + courier + ", regNo=" + regNo + "]"; 
 } 
 //Business Logic  
 public String shopping(String[] items,Float[] prices) 
 { 
  System.out.println("Flipkart.shopping()"); 
  System.out.println(courier.getClass().getName()); 
  String res = ""; 
  try { 
    Random random =null; 
    float bill = 0.0f; 
    int oid =0; 
    for(float price : prices) 
    { 
     bill+=price; 
    } 
    random = new Random(); 
    oid = random.nextInt(1000); 
    String msg = courier.deliver(oid); 
    res = Arrays.toString(items) + "are Purchased haveing Prices "+Arrays.toString(prices) 
    +" with bill Amount :: "+bill+" <----> "+msg; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return res; 
 } 
}

package com.Spring.StereoAnnotationMainApp; 
import org.springframework.context.support.ClassPathXmlApplicationContext; 
import com.Spring.StereoAnnotationsTarget.Flipkart; 
public class AutowireingMain { 
 static String path = 
"com/Spring/StereoAnnotationsAppConfig/AnnoatationAutowireingAppContext.xml"; 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  ClassPathXmlApplicationContext appcontext = new ClassPathXmlApplicationContext(path); 
  Flipkart flipKart = appcontext.getBean("fpkt", Flipkart.class); 
  String result = flipKart.shopping(new String[] {"Noise Smart Band","Puma","Iphone"}, new 
Float[] 
    {3123.33f,1500.65f,64999.56f}); 
  long regNumber= 0; 
  try { 
   regNumber = flipKart.getRegNo(); 
   System.out.println("Reg No : "+regNumber+result); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   System.out.println("Reg No : is Not Avalible...."); 
  } 
  if(regNumber<=0 || Long.valueOf(regNumber)==null) 
  { 
   System.out.println(result); 
  } 
  appcontext.close(); 
 } 
}

package com.Spring.StereoAnnotationsTarget; 
import java.util.Arrays; 
import java.util.Date; 
import java.util.Random; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Qualifier; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.PropertySource; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Scope; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.Spring.StereoAnnotations.Courier; 
@Component(value="fpkt") 
@Scope(scopeName = "prototype") 
@PropertySource(value= {"com/Spring/StereoAppProperties/Application.Properties"}) 
public class Flipkart { 
 //Feild level Autowireing ... 
 @Autowired 
 @Qualifier("newRef") 
 private Courier courier; 
 private Long regNo; 
 @Autowired 
 private Date date; 
 @Value("${fpkt.info.url}") 
 private String url; 
 @Value("${fpkt.info.discount}") 
 private int discount; 
 @Value("${Path}") 
 private String path; 
 @Value("${os.name}") 
 private String os; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("Flipkart.class file is loading..."); 
 } 
 public Flipkart() 
 { 
  System.out.println("Flipkart object is created..."); 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "Flipkart [courier=" + courier + ", regNo=" + regNo + "]"; 
 } 
 //Business Logic  
 public String shopping(String[] items,Float[] prices) 
 { 
  System.out.println("Flipkart.shopping()"); 
  System.out.println(courier.getClass().getName()); 
  System.out.println("Date object details :: " + date); 
  System.out.println("URL value is :: " + url); 
  System.out.println("Discount amount is :: " + discount); 
  System.out.println(); 
  System.out.println(os); 
  System.out.println(path); 
  String res = ""; 
  try { 
    Random random =null; 
    float bill = 0.0f; 
    int oid =0; 
    for(float price : prices) 
    { 
     bill+=price; 
    } 
    random = new Random(); 
    oid = random.nextInt(1000); 
    String msg = courier.deliver(oid); 
    res = Arrays.toString(items) + "are Purchased haveing Prices "+Arrays.toString(prices) 
    +" with bill Amount :: "+bill+" <----> "+msg; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return res; 
 } 
} 
Annotations used for lazy loading, keeping the beans in particular scope, and getting values from properties file: 
@Lazy --- On the bean it would perform Lazy Loading 
@Scope --- It specifies the scope in which the bean should be kept. 
@PropertySource(value="") --- It specifies the location from where the properties 
file data should be taken.

package com.Spring.TestMain; 
import java.util.Scanner; 
import org.springframework.context.support.ClassPathXmlApplicationContext; 
import com.Spring.Controller.CustomerController; 
import com.Spring.CustomerVo.CustomerVo; 
public class CustomerMain { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  ClassPathXmlApplicationContext appContext = new 
ClassPathXmlApplicationContext("com/Spring/Config/applicationContext.xml"); 
  CustomerController controller = appContext.getBean("controller", CustomerController.class);  
  CustomerVo vo = InserCustomerData(); 
  String result1 =controller.processResult(vo); 
  System.out.println(result1); 
  System.out.println("\t"); 
  int cid = getCustomerInfo(); 
  String result = controller.GetCustomerInfoById(cid); 
  System.out.println(result); 
 } 
 public static CustomerVo  InserCustomerData() 
 { 
  Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Name :: "); 
  String customerName = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Address :: "); 
  String customerAddress = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Amount :: "); 
  String customerAmount = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Time Period :: "); 
  String time = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Rate of Interest :: "); 
  String rate = sc.nextLine(); 
  CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
  vo.setCustomeraddress(customerAddress); 
  vo.setCustomerName(customerName); 
  vo.setPrincipleAmount(customerAmount); 
  vo.setTime(time); 
  vo.setRate(rate); 
  return vo; 
 } 
 public static int getCustomerInfo() 
 { 
  Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Id :: "); 
  int CID = sc.nextInt(); 
  return CID; 
 } 
} 
package com.Spring.Controller; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.Spring.CustomerVo.CustomerVo; 
import com.Spring.DTO.CustomerDto; 
import com.Spring.Service.CustomerMgmtService; 
@Component(value="controller") 
public class CustomerController { 
 @Autowired 
 CustomerMgmtService service; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerController  class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerController(CustomerMgmtService service) 
 { 
  System.out.println("Main Controller:: one param Constructor...!"); 
  this.service = service; 
 } 
 public String processResult(CustomerVo vo) 
 { 
  String Result =""; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   dto.setCustomerName(vo.getCustomerName()); 
   dto.setCustomeraddress(vo.getCustomeraddress()); 
   dto.setPrincipleAmount(Float.parseFloat(vo.getPrincipleAmount())); 
   dto.setRate(Float.parseFloat(vo.getRate())); 
   dto.setTime(Float.parseFloat(vo.getTime())); 
   String result = service.CalculateSimpleInterest(dto); 
   Result = result; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return Result; 
 } 
 public String GetCustomerInfoById(int id) 
 { 
  String result =""; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   result = service.getCustomerInfo(id); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return result; 
 } 
} 
package com.Spring.Service; 
import com.Spring.DTO.CustomerDto; 
public interface CustomerMgmtService { 
    public String CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerDto dto); 
    public String getCustomerInfo(int id); 
}

package com.Spring.Service; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service; 
import com.Spring.BO.CustomerBo; 
import com.Spring.DAO.CustomerDao; 
import com.Spring.DTO.CustomerDto; 
@Service(value="service") 
public class CustomerMgmtServiceImpl implements CustomerMgmtService { 
 @Autowired 
 private CustomerDao dao; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerMgmtServiceImpl class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerMgmtServiceImpl(CustomerDao dao) 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerMgmtServiceImpl:: 1 Param Constructor....!"); 
  this.dao = dao; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerDto dto) { 
  Float interestAmount = 0.0f; 
  String message =""; 
  try { 
   interestAmount= (dto.getPrincipleAmount()*dto.getTime()*dto.getRate())/100f; 
   CustomerBo bo  = new CustomerBo(); 
   bo.setCustomerName(dto.getCustomerName()); 
   bo.setCustomeraddress(dto.getCustomeraddress()); 
   bo.setPrincipleAmount(dto.getPrincipleAmount()); 
   bo.setRate(dto.getRate()); 
   bo.setTime(dto.getTime()); 
   int count =dao.Insert(bo); 
   if(count==0) 
   { 
    message = "Customer Regstration is Failed :: "+dto.getPrincipleAmount()+" Interest Amount Rate :: 
"+interestAmount; 
   }else 
   { 
    message = "Customer Regstration is Sucessfully :: "+dto.getPrincipleAmount()+" Interest Amount Rate 
:: "+interestAmount; 
   } 
   System.out.println("Message :: "+message); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return message; 
 } 
 public float CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerBo bo) { 
  Float interestAmount = 0.0f; 
  String message =""; 
  try { 
   interestAmount= (bo.getPrincipleAmount()*bo.getTime()*bo.getRate())/100f; 
   if(interestAmount!=0) 
   { 
    message = "Customer Principle Amount :: "+bo.getPrincipleAmount()+" Interest Amount Rate :: 
"+interestAmount; 
   }else 
   { 
    message = "Customer Does not Exits"; 
   } 
   System.out.println("Message :: "+message); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return interestAmount; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String getCustomerInfo(int id) { 
  String customerInfo=""; 
  try { 
   CustomerBo customer =  dao.findByID(id); 
      if(customer!=null) { 
    float intrest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customer); 
    customer.setRateofInterstAmount(intrest); 
    customerInfo = customer.toString(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Info : "+customerInfo); 
      } 
      else 
      { 
       System.out.println("Customer does't Exits....!"); 
      } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerInfo; 
 } 
}

@Repository(value = "MySQLDAO") 
public class CustomerMySQLDAOImp implements 
ICustomerDAO { 
 @Autowired 
 private DataSource dataSource;

package com.Spring.DAO; 
import com.Spring.BO.CustomerBo; 
public interface CustomerDao { 
 public  int Insert(CustomerBo bo); 
 public CustomerBo findByID(int id); 
} 
package com.Spring.DAO; 
import java.sql.Connection; 
import java.sql.PreparedStatement; 
import java.sql.ResultSet; 
import java.sql.SQLException; 
import javax.sql.DataSource; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Repository; 
import com.Spring.BO.CustomerBo; 
@Repository(value="MySQLDAO") 
public class CustomerMySQLDAOImpl implements CustomerDao {  
 private static final String Insert_Query = "Insert Into 
Spring_Customers(Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time) Values (?,?,?,?,?)"; 
 private static final String SelectBYID_Query= "select 
Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time from testschema.Spring_Customers where CID = ?"; 
 @Autowired 
 private DataSource datasource; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerDAOImpl class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerMySQLDAOImpl(DataSource datasource) { 
  System.out.println("CustomerDAOImpl :: 1 param Constructor..."); 
  this.datasource = datasource; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public int Insert(CustomerBo bo) { 
  int count = 0; 
  try { 
   Connection connection = datasource.getConnection(); 
   System.out.println("Connection Estiblished Sucessfully...."); 
   PreparedStatement prepareStatement = connection.prepareStatement(Insert_Query); 
   prepareStatement.setString(1, bo.getCustomerName()); 
   prepareStatement.setString(2, bo.getCustomeraddress()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(3, bo.getPrincipleAmount()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(4, bo.getRate()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(5, bo.getTime()); 
   count = prepareStatement.executeUpdate(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return count; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public CustomerBo findByID(int id) { 
  CustomerBo customer = null; 
  try { 
   Connection connection = datasource.getConnection(); 
   PreparedStatement prepareStatement = connection.prepareStatement(SelectBYID_Query); 
   prepareStatement.setInt(1, id); 
   ResultSet resultset = prepareStatement.executeQuery(); 
   while(resultset.next()) 
   { 
    customer = new CustomerBo(); 
    customer.setCustomerName(resultset.getString(1)); 
    customer.setCustomeraddress(resultset.getString(2)); 
    customer.setPrincipleAmount(resultset.getFloat(3)); 
    customer.setRate(resultset.getFloat(4)); 
    customer.setTime(resultset.getFloat(5)); 
   } 
  }catch (SQLException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customer; 
 } 
}

✅ @PostConstruct 
When is it called? 
➡️ Immediately after the bean is initialized by the Spring container — after constructor, after properties (setters or 
autowiring) are injected. 
Why use it? 
➡️ To perform custom initialization logic like: 
 Validating input fields 
 Initializing helper objects 
 Preparing resources 
✅ @PreDestroy 
When is it called? 
➡️ Right before the bean is destroyed (when the Spring container shuts down or bean is manually removed). 
Why use it? 
➡️ To perform clean-up tasks, like: 
 Releasing resources 
 Closing connections 
 Nullifying sensitive data 
Java Class vs Spring Bean Lifecycle 
Java Class Lifecycle Spring Bean Lifecycle 
Static Block – Executes 
once on class load 
Static Block – Executes once on class 
load 
Instance Block – Runs 
before constructor 
Not applicable directly (handled by 
Spring) 
Constructor – Object is 
created 
Object Instantiation – Spring creates 
the bean 
Setters – Inject values 
manually 
Dependency Injection – Done by 
Spring 
Manual Method Call – 
You invoke business 
methods 
@PostConstruct – Custom init method 
runs 
✔ If successful → business methods 
are used 
Business Logic Execution Business Logic Execution 
Garbage Collection – 
JVM cleans the object 
@PreDestroy – Custom cleanup before 
bean removal 
❌ No explicit control on 
destruction timing 
✅ Controlled by Spring container 
shutdown 
package com.Voter.verification; 
import java.util.Date; 
//JDK9 supplied annotations, not from SpringFramework 
import javax.annotation.PostConstruct; 
import javax.annotation.PreDestroy; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.PropertySource; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
@Component(value = "voterVerification") 
@PropertySource(value="com/Voters/Config/Voter.Properties") 
public class VoterVerification { 
 @Value("${voterVerifier.name}") 
 private String name; 
 @Value("${voterVerifier.age}") 
 private float age; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("VoterVerifier.class file is loading...."); 
 } 
 public VoterVerification() { 
  System.out.println("VoterVerifier object is instantiated..."); 
 } 
 private Date dateVerification; 
 public String getName() { 
  return name; 
 } 
 public void setName(String name) { 
  this.name = name; 
 } 
 public float getAge() { 
  return age; 
 } 
 public void setAge(float age) { 
  this.age = age; 
 } 
 public Date getDateVerification() { 
  return dateVerification; 
 } 
 public void setDateVerification(Date dateVerification) { 
  this.dateVerification = dateVerification; 
 } 
 @PostConstruct 
 public void ourInit() { 
  System.out.println("VoterVerifier.outInit():: custom init method"); 
  dateVerification = new Date(); 
  if (name == null || age < 0) 
   throw new IllegalArgumentException("invalid inputs are given for name,age properties of a 
bean"); 
 } 
 public String checkEligibility() { 
  if (age < 18) { 
   return "Mr/Miss/Mrs " + name + " u r not eligible for voting.... wait " + (18 - age) 
     + "  years to cast ur vote on -->" + dateVerification; 
  } else { 
   return "Mr/Miss/Mrs " + name + " u r  eligible for voting.... Do not wait on --->" + 
dateVerification; 
  } 
 } 
 @PreDestroy 
 public void ourDestroy() { 
  System.out.println("VoterVerifier.ourDestroy():: custom destroy method"); 
  // nullify bean properties 
  name = null; 
  age = 0.0f; 
  dateVerification = null; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "VoterVerifier [name=" + name + ", age=" + age + ", dateVerification=" + dateVerification + 
"]"; 
 } 
}

Spring XML Configuration Summary 
1. applicationContext.xml 
Acts as the central configuration file. 
Imports: 
 controller-beans.xml 
 service-beans.xml 
 persistence-beans.xml 
2. controller-beans.xml 
 Defines CustomerController bean. 
 Injects serviceImpl (service layer dependency). 
3. service-beans.xml 
Defines CustomerMgmtServiceImpl as serviceImpl. 
Injects mysqlDaoImpl (DAO layer dependency). 
4. persistence-beans.xml 
Loads properties from application.properties. 
Configures: 
 mysqlDataSource (basic DB config). 
 hikariDataSource (advanced connection pool). 
 CustomerMySQLDAOImp as mysqlDaoImpl (DAO). 
 Injects hikariDataSource into DAO.

 In layered apporach,having all the information of controller,service,dao in single xml file is not 
recomended,becoz it disturbs the readablity if the projet is lengthy project.To avoid this we 
need to seperate the xml configuration details w.r.t layers and all these layers are linked in 
single xml file.To do this we use a tag called <import resource = ''/> 
package com.TestMain; 
import java.util.Scanner; 
import org.springframework.context.support.ClassPathXmlApplicationContext; 
import com.CustomerVo.CustomerVo; 
import com.SpringController.CustomerController; 
public class CustomerMain { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  ClassPathXmlApplicationContext appContext = new 
ClassPathXmlApplicationContext("com/SpringConfig/applicationcontext.xml"); 
  CustomerController controller = appContext.getBean("controller", 
CustomerController.class); 
//  CustomerVo vo = InserCustomerData(); 
//  String result =controller.processResult(vo); 
  int cid = getCustomerInfo(); 
  String result = controller.GetCustomerInfoById(cid); 
 } 
 public static CustomerVo  InserCustomerData() 
 { 
  Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Name :: "); 
  String customerName = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Address :: "); 
  String customerAddress = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Amount :: "); 
  String customerAmount = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Time Period :: "); 
  String time = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Rate of Interest :: "); 
  String rate = sc.nextLine(); 
  CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
  vo.setCustomeraddress(customerAddress); 
  vo.setCustomerName(customerName); 
  vo.setPrincipleAmount(customerAmount); 
  vo.setTime(time); 
  vo.setRate(rate); 
  return vo; 
 } 
 public static int getCustomerInfo() 
 { 
  Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Id :: "); 
  int CID = sc.nextInt(); 
  return CID; 
 } 
}

Dependency Injection (DI) using XML + Annotation in Spring:- 
 Dependency Injection (DI) using XML + Annotation in Spring is a hybrid configuration approach 
where XML is used to define and wire beans, while annotations like @Component, 
@Autowired, and @Repository are used inside Java classes to mark and inject dependencies. 
This setup enables loose coupling and separation of concerns, and is often used in database CRUD 
operations by wiring DAO, Service, and Controller layers. 
Spring uses XML to load the application context, scan component classes, and manage bean life 
cycles, while annotations streamline dependency injection and class identification. 
Presentance Bean.xml: 
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?> 
<beans xmlns="http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans" 
 xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" 
 xmlns:context="http://www.springframework.org/schema/context" 
 xsi:schemaLocation="http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans 
        https://www.springframework.org/schema/beans/spring-beans.xsd 
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/context 
        https://www.springframework.org/schema/context/spring-context.xsd"> 
 <!-- Load properties file --> 
    <bean id="properties" 
class="org.springframework.beans.factory.config.PropertyPlaceholderConfigurer"> 
        <property name="location" value="classpath:com/SpringJDBCProperties/application.properties"/> 
    </bean> 
    <!-- Data Source Configuration --> 
    <bean id="mysqlDataSource" class="org.springframework.jdbc.datasource.DriverManagerDataSource"> 
        <property name="driverClassName" value="${jdbc.driver}"/> 
        <property name="username" value="${jdbc.user}"/> 
        <property name="password" value="${jdbc.password}"/>  
    </bean> 
    <!-- Add primary="true" to hikariDataSource --> 
 <bean id="hikariDataSource" class="com.zaxxer.hikari.HikariDataSource" parent="mysqlDataSource" 
primary="true"> 
     <property name="jdbcUrl" value="${jdbc.url}"/> 
     <property name="minimumIdle" value="10"/> 
     <property name="maximumPoolSize" value="20"/> 
     <property name="connectionTimeout" value="2000"/> 
 </bean> 
</beans>

package com.CustomerVo; 
public class CustomerVo { 
 private String customerName; 
 private String customeraddress; 
 private String principleAmount; 
 private String rate; 
 private String time; 
 private String RateofInterstAmount; 
 public String getRateofInterstAmount() { 
  return RateofInterstAmount; 
 } 
 public void setRateofInterstAmount(String rateofInterstAmount) { 
  RateofInterstAmount = rateofInterstAmount; 
 } 
 public String getCustomerName() { 
  return customerName; 
 } 
 public void setCustomerName(String customerName) { 
  this.customerName = customerName; 
 } 
 public String getCustomeraddress() { 
  return customeraddress; 
 } 
 public void setCustomeraddress(String customeraddress) { 
  this.customeraddress = customeraddress; 
 } 
 public String getPrincipleAmount() { 
  return principleAmount; 
 } 
 public void setPrincipleAmount(String principleAmount) { 
  this.principleAmount = principleAmount; 
 } 
 public String getRate() { 
  return rate; 
 } 
 public void setRate(String rate) { 
  this.rate = rate; 
 } 
 public String getTime() { 
  return time; 
 } 
 public void setTime(String time) { 
  this.time = time; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "CustomerVo [customerName=" + customerName + ", 
customeraddress=" + customeraddress 
    + ", principleAmount=" + principleAmount + ", rate=" + 
rate + ", time=" + time + ", RateofInterstAmount=" + RateofInterstAmount + "]"; 
 } 
}

package com.SpringDAO; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.SpringBO.CustomerBo; 
public interface CustomerDao { 
 public  int Insert(CustomerBo bo); 
 public CustomerBo findByID(int id); 
 public List<CustomerBo> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
} 
package com.SpringDAO; 
import java.sql.Connection; 
import java.sql.PreparedStatement; 
import java.sql.ResultSet; 
import java.sql.SQLException; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import javax.sql.DataSource; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Repository; 
import com.SpringBO.CustomerBo; 
@Repository("dao") 
public class CustomerDAOImpl implements CustomerDao {  
 private static final String Insert_Query = "Insert Into 
Spring_Customers(Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time) Values (?,?,?,?,?)"; 
 private static final String SelectBYID_Query= "select Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time from 
testschema.Spring_Customers where CID = ?"; 
 private static final String SelectAll_Query = "select Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time from 
testschema.Spring_Customers"; 
 @Autowired 
 //@Qualifier(value = "hikariDataSource") 
 private DataSource datasource; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerDAOImpl class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerDAOImpl(DataSource datasource) { 
  System.out.println("CustomerDAOImpl :: 1 param Constructor..."); 
  this.datasource = datasource; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public int Insert(CustomerBo bo) { 
  int count = 0; 
  try { 
   Connection connection = datasource.getConnection(); 
   System.out.println("Connection Estiblished Sucessfully...."); 
   PreparedStatement prepareStatement = connection.prepareStatement(Insert_Query); 
   prepareStatement.setString(1, bo.getCustomerName()); 
   prepareStatement.setString(2, bo.getCustomeraddress()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(3, bo.getPrincipleAmount()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(4, bo.getRate()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(5, bo.getTime()); 
   count = prepareStatement.executeUpdate(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return count; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public CustomerBo findByID(int id) { 
  CustomerBo customer = null; 
  try { 
   Connection connection = datasource.getConnection(); 
   PreparedStatement prepareStatement = connection.prepareStatement(SelectBYID_Query); 
   prepareStatement.setInt(1, id); 
   ResultSet resultset = prepareStatement.executeQuery(); 
   while(resultset.next()) 
   { 
    customer = new CustomerBo(); 
    customer.setCustomerName(resultset.getString(1)); 
    customer.setCustomeraddress(resultset.getString(2)); 
    customer.setPrincipleAmount(resultset.getFloat(3)); 
    customer.setRate(resultset.getFloat(4)); 
    customer.setTime(resultset.getFloat(5)); 
   } 
  }catch (SQLException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customer; 
 } 
@Override 
 public List<CustomerBo> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  CustomerBo customer = null; 
  List<CustomerBo> customerBoList = new ArrayList<CustomerBo>(); 
  try(Connection connection = datasource.getConnection()) { 
   PreparedStatement prepareStatement = connection.prepareStatement(SelectAll_Query); 
   ResultSet resultset = prepareStatement.executeQuery(); 
   //customerBoList = new ArrayList<CustomerBo>(); 
   while(resultset.next()) 
   { 
    customer = new CustomerBo(); 
    customer.setCustomerName(resultset.getString(1)); 
    customer.setCustomeraddress(resultset.getString(2)); 
    customer.setPrincipleAmount(resultset.getFloat(3)); 
    customer.setRate(resultset.getFloat(4)); 
    customer.setTime(resultset.getFloat(5)); 
    //Adding to the List.. 
    customerBoList.add(customer); 
   } 
  }  
  catch (SQLException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerBoList; 
 } 
}

package com.SpringService; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.SpringDTO.CustomerDto; 
public interface CustomerMgmtService { 
    public String CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerDto dto); 
    public String getCustomerInfo(int id); 
    public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
} 
package com.SpringService; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service; 
import com.SpringBO.CustomerBo; 
import com.SpringDAO.CustomerDao; 
import com.SpringDTO.CustomerDto; 
@Service("service") 
public class CustomerMgmtServiceImpl implements CustomerMgmtService { 
 @Autowired 
 private CustomerDao dao; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerMgmtServiceImpl class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerMgmtServiceImpl(CustomerDao dao) 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerMgmtServiceImpl:: 1 Param Constructor....!"); 
  this.dao = dao; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerDto dto) { 
  Float interestAmount = 0.0f; 
  String message =""; 
  try { 
   interestAmount= (dto.getPrincipleAmount()*dto.getTime()*dto.getRate())/100f; 
   CustomerBo bo  = new CustomerBo(); 
   bo.setCustomerName(dto.getCustomerName()); 
   bo.setCustomeraddress(dto.getCustomeraddress()); 
   bo.setPrincipleAmount(dto.getPrincipleAmount()); 
   bo.setRate(dto.getRate()); 
   bo.setTime(dto.getTime()); 
   int count =dao.Insert(bo); 
   if(count==0) 
   { 
    message = "Customer Regstration is Failed :: "+dto.getPrincipleAmount()+" Interest 
Amount Rate :: "+interestAmount; 
   }else 
   { 
    message = "Customer Regstration is Sucessfully :: "+dto.getPrincipleAmount()+" 
Interest Amount Rate :: "+interestAmount; 
   } 
   System.out.println("Message :: "+message); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return message; 
 } 
 public float CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerBo bo) { 
  Float interestAmount = 0.0f; 
  String message =""; 
  try { 
   interestAmount= (bo.getPrincipleAmount()*bo.getTime()*bo.getRate())/100f; 
   if(interestAmount!=0) 
   { 
    message = "Customer Principle Amount :: "+bo.getPrincipleAmount()+" Interest Amount 
Rate :: "+interestAmount; 
   }else 
   { 
    message = "Customer Does not Exits"; 
   } 
   System.out.println("Message :: "+message); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return interestAmount; 
 } 
@Override 
 public String getCustomerInfo(int id) { 
  String customerInfo=""; 
  try { 
   CustomerBo customer =  dao.findByID(id); 
      if(customer!=null) { 
    float intrest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customer); 
    customer.setRateofInterstAmount(intrest); 
    customerInfo = customer.toString(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Info : "+customerInfo); 
      } 
      else 
      { 
       System.out.println("Customer does't Exits....!"); 
      } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerInfo; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerDto> customerDtoList = new ArrayList<CustomerDto>(); 
  try { 
   List<CustomerBo> customerBoList = dao.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
   for(CustomerBo customerBo :  customerBoList) 
   { 
    CustomerDto customer = new CustomerDto(); 
    customer.setCustomerName(customerBo.getCustomerName()); 
    customer.setCustomeraddress(customerBo.getCustomeraddress()); 
    customer.setPrincipleAmount(customerBo.getRateofInterstAmount()); 
    customer.setRate(customerBo.getRate()); 
    customer.setTime(customerBo.getTime()); 
    float interest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customerBo); 
    customer.setRateofInterstAmount(interest); 
    customerDtoList.add(customer); 
   } 
  }  
  catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerDtoList; 
 } 
}

package com.SpringController; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.CustomerVo.CustomerVo; 
import com.SpringDTO.CustomerDto; 
import com.SpringService.CustomerMgmtService; 
@Component("controller") 
public class CustomerController implements CustomerControllerInterface{ 
 @Autowired 
 CustomerMgmtService service; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerController  class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerController(CustomerMgmtService service) 
 { 
  System.out.println("Main Controller:: one param Constructor...!"); 
  this.service = service; 
 } 
 public String processResult(CustomerVo vo) 
 { 
  String Result =""; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   dto.setCustomerName(vo.getCustomerName()); 
   dto.setCustomeraddress(vo.getCustomeraddress()); 
   dto.setPrincipleAmount(Float.parseFloat(vo.getPrincipleAmount())); 
   dto.setRate(Float.parseFloat(vo.getRate())); 
   dto.setTime(Float.parseFloat(vo.getTime())); 
   String result = service.CalculateSimpleInterest(dto); 
   Result = result; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return Result; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String findById(int id) 
 { 
  String result =""; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   result = service.getCustomerInfo(id); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return result; 
 }
@Override 
 public List<CustomerVo> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerDto> customerDtoList = service.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
  List<CustomerVo> customerVoList = new ArrayList<CustomerVo>(); 
  try { 
   for(CustomerDto customerdto : customerDtoList) 
   { 
    CustomerVo Customervo = new CustomerVo(); 
    Customervo.setCustomerName(customerdto.getCustomerName()); 
 Customervo.setPrincipleAmount(String.valueOf(customerdto.getPrincipleAmount())); 
    Customervo.setRate(String.valueOf(customerdto.getRate())); 
    Customervo.setCustomeraddress(customerdto.getCustomeraddress()); 
    Customervo.setTime(String.valueOf(customerdto.getTime())); 
 Customervo.setRateofInterstAmount(String.valueOf(customerdto.getRateofInterstAmount())); 
    customerVoList.add(Customervo); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerVoList; 
 } 
}

The p-namespace and c-namespace in Spring XML are syntactic shortcuts introduced to simplify property and 
constructor injection in bean definitions. 
However, they come with notable limitations that reduce their flexibility and usefulness in complex scenarios. 
These limitations include: 
1. Lack of support for collection injection – p-namespace does not support injecting lists, sets, or maps, 
which are common in real-world configurations. 
2. No resolution for constructor ambiguity – c-namespace cannot disambiguate constructor arguments by 
type, index, or order, which is necessary when constructors are overloaded. 
3. Outdated approach – Both namespaces were introduced late, at a time when the Java ecosystem was 
rapidly adopting annotation-based configuration (@Autowired, @Component, etc.), making them less 
relevant and rarely used in modern Spring applications. 
 ApllicationContext.xml: 
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?> 
<beans xmlns="http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans" 
 xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" 
 xmlns:p="http://www.springframework.org/schema/p" 
 xmlns:c="http://www.springframework.org/schema/c" 
 xsi:schemaLocation="http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans 
        https://www.springframework.org/schema/beans/spring-beans.xsd 
        http://www.springframework.org/schema/context 
        https://www.springframework.org/schema/context/spring-context.xsd"> 
 <bean id="dob" class="java.util.Date"> 
  <property name="date" value="03" /> 
  <property name="month" value="0" /> 
  <property name="year" value="93" /> 
 </bean> 
 <bean id="dos" class="java.util.Date" p:month="02" p:date="25" 
  p:year="123" /> 
 <bean id="emp" class="com.Spring_PandC_NameSpaceing.Employee" p:eno="10" 
  p:ename="sachin" p:dob-ref="dob" p:dept-ref="dept" /> 
 <bean id="dept" class="com.Spring_PandC_NameSpaceing.Department" c:dno="10" 
  c:dname="CS" c:dos-ref="dos"/> 
</beans> 
package com.Spring_PandC_NameSpaceing; 
import java.util.Date; 
public class Department { 
 private int dno; 
 private String dname; 
 private Date dos; 
 public Department(int dno, String dname, Date dos) { 
  System.out.println("Constructor : Constructor Injection..."); 
  this.dno = dno; 
  this.dname = dname; 
  this.dos = dos; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "Department [dno=" + dno + ", dname=" + dname + ", dos=" 
+ dos + "]"; 
 } 
}

Pure Java Configuration / 100% Code-Driven Spring App Development / Java Config Approach: 
 Pure Java Configuration (also known as Java-based Configuration or 100% Code-Driven Spring 
Application Development) is a modern approach to building Spring applications without using any XML 
configuration. 
 Instead of defining beans in an XML file, all configurations are done using Java classes and annotations, 
such as @Configuration, @Bean, and @ComponentScan. 
This approach enhances type safety, readability, and maintainability, and forms the foundation of Spring 
Boot. 
Implementation Class Used In 
FileSystemXmlApplicationContext Standalone apps (XML config) 
ClassPathXmlApplicationContext Standalone apps (XML config) 
XmlWebApplicationContext Spring MVC apps (XML config) 
AnnotationConfigApplicationContext Standalone apps (Java config) 
AnnotationConfigWebApplicationContext Spring MVC apps (Java config) 
Advantages of Java-Based Configuration: 
 🚫 No need for XML configuration 
 👁️🗨️ Improved code readability 
 🐞 Easier to debug and maintain 
 🚀 Acts as the foundation for Spring Boot 
Java Config Thumb Rules 
S.number Rule Description 
1. Annotate user-defined classes with stereotype annotations like @Component 
 Use @ComponentScan in the @Configuration class to detect them 
2. Define predefined (library) classes as Spring beans using @Bean methods 
 These methods should be inside a class annotated with @Configuration 
3. Use AnnotationConfigApplicationContext to bootstrap the Spring container 
 Pass the @Configuration class name as an argument 
package com.Spring.PureCodeDriven; 
import java.time.LocalDateTime; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.ComponentScan; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Configuration; 
@Configuration 
@ComponentScan(basePackages = "com.Spring") 
public class AppConfig { 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("App Config Class is Loading..."); 
 } 
 public AppConfig() 
 { 
  System.out.println("App Config Object is Created: Zero Param Constructor..."); 
 } 
 @Bean(name ="dt") 
 public LocalDateTime getSystemDateTime() 
 { 
  System.out.println("AppConfig.getSysDateTime()"); 
  LocalDateTime time = LocalDateTime.now(); 
  return time; 
 } 
} 
package com.Spring.PureCodeDriven; 
import java.time.LocalDateTime; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
@Component(value = "Wmg") 
public class MessageGenerator { 
 static { 
  System.out.println("MessageGenerator.class file is loading..."); 
 } 
 public MessageGenerator() { 
  System.out.println("MessageGenerator Object is Created: Zero Param Constructor..."); 
 } 
 @Autowired 
 private LocalDateTime date; 
 public String getMessage(String User) 
 { 
  int hour = date.getHour(); 
  if (hour >=6 && hour<=12) { 
   return "Hello :: " + User + " Good Morning "; 
  } else if (hour >=12 &&hour <= 16) { 
   return "Hello :: " + User + " Good Afternoon "; 
  } else if (hour >=16 && hour <= 20) { 
   return"Hello :: " + User + " Good Evening "; 
  } else { 
   return "Hello :: " + User + " Good Night "; 
  } 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() 
 { 
  return "MessageGenerator [date=" + date + "]"; 
 } 
} 
package com.Spring.PureCodeDriven; 
import org.springframework.context.ApplicationContext; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.AnnotationConfigApplicationContext; 
import org.springframework.context.support.AbstractApplicationContext; 
public class Test_MessageGenerator { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  ApplicationContext context = new AnnotationConfigApplicationContext(AppConfig.class); 
  System.out.println("*****Container started*******\n"); 
  MessageGenerator message = context.getBean(MessageGenerator.class); 
  System.out.println(message); 
  String msg = message.getMessage("Teja"); 
  System.out.println(msg); 
  ((AbstractApplicationContext) context).close(); 
  System.out.println("\n*****Container closed*******"); 
 } 
}

package com.SpringController; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.CustomerVo.CustomerVo; 
import com.SpringDTO.CustomerDto; 
import com.SpringService.CustomerMgmtService; 
@Component("controller") 
public class CustomerController implements CustomerControllerInterface{ 
 @Autowired 
 CustomerMgmtService service; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerController  class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerController(CustomerMgmtService service) 
 { 
  System.out.println("Main Controller:: one param Constructor...!"); 
  this.service = service; 
 } 
 public String processResult(CustomerVo vo) 
 { 
  String Result =""; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   dto.setCustomerName(vo.getCustomerName()); 
   dto.setCustomeraddress(vo.getCustomeraddress()); 
   dto.setPrincipleAmount(Float.parseFloat(vo.getPrincipleAmount())); 
   dto.setRate(Float.parseFloat(vo.getRate())); 
   dto.setTime(Float.parseFloat(vo.getTime())); 
   String result = service.CalculateSimpleInterest(dto); 
   Result = result; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return Result; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String findById(int id) 
 { 
  String result =""; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   result = service.getCustomerInfo(id); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return result; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerVo> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerDto> customerDtoList = service.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
  List<CustomerVo> customerVoList = new ArrayList<CustomerVo>(); 
  try { 
   for(CustomerDto customerdto : customerDtoList) 
   { 
    CustomerVo Customervo = new CustomerVo(); 
    Customervo.setCustomerName(customerdto.getCustomerName()); 
    Customervo.setPrincipleAmount(String.valueOf(customerdto.getPrincipleAmount())); 
    Customervo.setRate(String.valueOf(customerdto.getRate())); 
    Customervo.setCustomeraddress(customerdto.getCustomeraddress()); 
    Customervo.setTime(String.valueOf(customerdto.getTime())); 
 Customervo.setRateofInterstAmount(String.valueOf(customerdto.getRateofInterstAmount())); 
    customerVoList.add(Customervo); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerVoList; 
 } 
}

package com.SpringDTO; 
public class CustomerDto { 
 private String customerName; 
 private String customeraddress; 
 private Float principleAmount; 
 private Float rate; 
 private Float time; 
 private Float RateofInterstAmount; 
 public Float getRateofInterstAmount() { 
  return RateofInterstAmount; 
 } 
 public void setRateofInterstAmount(Float rateofInterstAmount) { 
  RateofInterstAmount = rateofInterstAmount;

package com.SpringService; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.SpringDTO.CustomerDto; 
public interface CustomerMgmtService { 
    public String CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerDto dto); 
    public String getCustomerInfo(int id); 
    public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
} 
Service Interface(CustomerMgmtService) 
) 
package com.SpringService; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service; 
import com.SpringBO.CustomerBo; 
import com.SpringDAO.CustomerDao; 
import com.SpringDTO.CustomerDto; 
@Service("service") 
public class CustomerMgmtServiceImpl implements CustomerMgmtService { 
 @Autowired 
 private CustomerDao dao; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("CustomerMgmtServiceImpl class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerMgmtServiceImpl(CustomerDao dao) { 
  System.out.println("CustomerMgmtServiceImpl:: 1 Param Constructor....!"); 
  this.dao = dao; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerDto dto) { 
  Float interestAmount = 0.0f; 
  String message = ""; 
  try { 
   interestAmount = (dto.getPrincipleAmount() * dto.getTime() * dto.getRate()) / 100f; 
   CustomerBo bo = new CustomerBo(); 
   bo.setCustomerName(dto.getCustomerName()); 
   bo.setCustomeraddress(dto.getCustomeraddress()); 
   bo.setPrincipleAmount(dto.getPrincipleAmount()); 
   bo.setRate(dto.getRate()); 
   bo.setTime(dto.getTime()); 
   int count = dao.Insert(bo); 
   if (count == 0) { 
    message = "Customer Regstration is Failed :: " + dto.getPrincipleAmount() + " Interest Amount Rate :: " 
      + interestAmount; 
   } else { 
    message = "Customer Regstration is Sucessfully :: " + dto.getPrincipleAmount() 
      + " Interest Amount Rate :: " + interestAmount; 
   } 
   System.out.println("Message :: " + message); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return message; 
 } 
 public float CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerBo bo) { 
  Float interestAmount = 0.0f; 
  String message = ""; 
  try { 
   interestAmount = (bo.getPrincipleAmount() * bo.getTime() * bo.getRate()) / 100f; 
   if (interestAmount != 0) { 
    message = "Customer Principle Amount :: " + bo.getPrincipleAmount() + " Interest Amount Rate :: " 
      + interestAmount; 
   } else { 
    message = "Customer Does not Exits"; 
   } 
   System.out.println("Message :: " + message); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return interestAmount; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String getCustomerInfo(int id) { 
  String customerInfo = ""; 
  try { 
   CustomerBo customer = dao.findByID(id); 
   if (customer != null) { 
    float intrest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customer); 
    customer.setRateofInterstAmount(intrest); 
    customerInfo = customer.toString(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Info : " + customerInfo); 
   } else { 
    System.out.println("Customer does't Exits....!"); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerInfo; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerDto> customerDtoList = new ArrayList<CustomerDto>(); 
  try { 
   List<CustomerBo> customerBoList = dao.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
   for (CustomerBo customerBo : customerBoList) { 
    CustomerDto customer = new CustomerDto(); 
    customer.setCustomerName(customerBo.getCustomerName()); 
    customer.setCustomeraddress(customerBo.getCustomeraddress()); 
    customer.setPrincipleAmount(customerBo.getRateofInterstAmount()); 
    customer.setRate(customerBo.getRate()); 
    customer.setTime(customerBo.getTime()); 
    float interest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customerBo); 
    customer.setRateofInterstAmount(interest); 
    customerDtoList.add(customer); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerDtoList; 
 } 
}

package com.SpringDAO;

CustomerDao Interface 
package com.SpringDAO; 
import java.sql.Connection; 
import java.sql.PreparedStatement; 
import java.sql.ResultSet; 
import java.sql.SQLException; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import javax.sql.DataSource; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Repository; 
import com.SpringBO.CustomerBo; 
@Repository("dao") 
public class CustomerDAOImpl implements CustomerDao { 
 private static final String Insert_Query = "Insert Into 
Spring_Customers(Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time) 
Values (?,?,?,?,?)"; 
 private static final String SelectBYID_Query = "select 
Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time from 
testschema.Spring_Customers where CID = ?"; 
 private static final String SelectAll_Query = "select 
Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time from 
testschema.Spring_Customers"; 
 @Autowired 
 // @Qualifier(value = "hikariDataSource") 
 private DataSource datasource; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("CustomerDAOImpl class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerDAOImpl(DataSource datasource) { 
  System.out.println("CustomerDAOImpl :: 1 param Constructor..."); 
  this.datasource = datasource; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public int Insert(CustomerBo bo) { 
  int count = 0; 
  try { 
   Connection connection = datasource.getConnection(); 
   System.out.println("Connection Estiblished Sucessfully...."); 
   PreparedStatement prepareStatement = 
connection.prepareStatement(Insert_Query); 
   prepareStatement.setString(1, bo.getCustomerName()); 
   prepareStatement.setString(2, bo.getCustomeraddress()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(3, bo.getPrincipleAmount()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(4, bo.getRate()); 
   prepareStatement.setFloat(5, bo.getTime()); 
   count = prepareStatement.executeUpdate(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return count; 
 } 
CustomerDAOImpl 
@Override 
public CustomerBo findByID(int id) { 
  CustomerBo customer = null; 
  try { 
   Connection connection = datasource.getConnection(); 
   PreparedStatement prepareStatement = 
connection.prepareStatement(SelectBYID_Query); 
   prepareStatement.setInt(1, id); 
   ResultSet resultset = prepareStatement.executeQuery(); 
   while (resultset.next()) { 
    customer = new CustomerBo(); 
    customer.setCustomerName(resultset.getString(1)); 
    customer.setCustomeraddress(resultset.getString(2)); 
    customer.setPrincipleAmount(resultset.getFloat(3)); 
    customer.setRate(resultset.getFloat(4)); 
    customer.setTime(resultset.getFloat(5)); 
   } 
  } catch (SQLException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customer; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerBo> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  CustomerBo customer = null; 
  List<CustomerBo> customerBoList = new ArrayList<CustomerBo>(); 
  try (Connection connection = datasource.getConnection()) { 
   PreparedStatement prepareStatement = 
connection.prepareStatement(SelectAll_Query); 
   ResultSet resultset = prepareStatement.executeQuery(); 
   // customerBoList = new ArrayList<CustomerBo>(); 
   while (resultset.next()) { 
    customer = new CustomerBo(); 
    customer.setCustomerName(resultset.getString(1)); 
    customer.setCustomeraddress(resultset.getString(2)); 
    customer.setPrincipleAmount(resultset.getFloat(3)); 
    customer.setRate(resultset.getFloat(4)); 
    customer.setTime(resultset.getFloat(5)); 
    // Adding to the List.. 
    customerBoList.add(customer); 
   } 
  } catch (SQLException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerBoList; 
 } 
}

Application.properties 
package com.SpringConfig; 
import javax.sql.DataSource; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Bean; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.ComponentScan; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.PropertySource; 
import org.springframework.core.env.Environment; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.zaxxer.hikari.HikariDataSource; 
@Component 
@ComponentScan(basePackages = "com") 
@PropertySource(value = "com/SpringJDBCProperties/application.properties") 
public class AppConfig { 
 @Autowired 
 private Environment environment; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("AppConfig Class is Loading..."); 
 } 
 public AppConfig() 
 { 
  System.out.println("AppConfig object is created :: Zero param constructor..."); 
 } 
 @Bean 
 public DataSource getDataSource() 
 { 
  System.out.println("Implementation class name of Environment is :: 
"+environment.getClass().getName()); 
  HikariDataSource dataSource = new HikariDataSource(); 
  dataSource.setDriverClassName(environment.getProperty("jdbc.driver")); 
  dataSource.setUsername(environment.getProperty("jdbc.user")); 
  dataSource.setPassword(environment.getProperty("jdbc.password")); 
  dataSource.setJdbcUrl(environment.getProperty("jdbc.url")); 
 dataSource.setMinimumIdle(Integer.parseInt(environment.getProperty("jdbc.pool.minidle"))); 
 dataSource.setMaximumPoolSize(Integer.parseInt(environment.getProperty("jdbc.pool.maxpoolsize")
)); 
 dataSource.setConnectionTimeout(Integer.parseInt(environment.getProperty("jdbc.pool.connectiont
imeout"))); 
  return dataSource; 
 } 
}

package com.TestMain; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.Scanner; 
import org.springframework.context.ApplicationContext; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.AnnotationConfigApplicationContext; 
import com.CustomerVo.CustomerVo; 
import com.SpringConfig.AppConfig; 
import com.SpringController.CustomerController; 
public class CustomerMain { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  ApplicationContext appContext = new AnnotationConfigApplicationContext(AppConfig.class); 
  CustomerController controller = appContext.getBean("controller", 
CustomerController.class); 
  CustomerVo vo = InserCustomerData(); 
  String result1 = controller.processResult(vo); 
  System.out.println(result1); 
  int cid = getCustomerInfo(); 
  String result = controller.findById(cid); 
  System.out.println(result); 
  List<CustomerVo> customerList = controller.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
  customerList.forEach(System.out::println); 
 } 
 public static CustomerVo InserCustomerData() { 
  Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Name :: "); 
  String customerName = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Address :: "); 
  String customerAddress = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Amount :: "); 
  String customerAmount = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Time Period :: "); 
  String time = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Rate of Interest :: "); 
  String rate = sc.nextLine(); 
  CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
  vo.setCustomeraddress(customerAddress); 
  vo.setCustomerName(customerName); 
  vo.setPrincipleAmount(customerAmount); 
  vo.setTime(time); 
  vo.setRate(rate); 
  return vo; 
 } 
 public static int getCustomerInfo() { 
  Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Id :: "); 
  int CID = sc.nextInt(); 
  return CID; 
 } 
}

This image guides beginners to correctly set up and locate key files in a Spring Boot project, 
ensuring the @SpringBootApplication class is in the root package and configurations are in 
src/main/resources. 
Spring Boot – Definition 
Spring Boot is a framework built on top of the Spring Framework that makes it easier and faster 
to develop Spring-based applications by providing auto-configuration, embedded servers 
(Tomcat, Jetty), and starter dependencies. 
It removes the need for much of the boilerplate configuration found in Spring, allowing you to 
focus on writing business logic instead of setup code. 
Feature / 
Point Spring Framework Spring Boot 
Definition A powerful, flexible framework for building Java applications. A tool built on top of Spring to make Spring application 
development faster and easier. 
Configuration Requires manual XML or Java-based configuration for beans, data sources, 
etc. 
Uses Auto-Configuration to set up most configurations 
automatically. 
Setup You need to configure servers and dependencies manually. 
Comes with embedded servers (Tomcat, Jetty, 
Undertow), so you can run applications without external 
deployment. 
Starter 
Dependencies No built-in starters; you must add each dependency yourself. 
Provides Spring Boot Starters — pre-packaged 
dependency sets for common features (web, JPA, 
security, etc.). 
Deployment Usually deployed on an external server (like Tomcat, WebLogic). Deployable as a standalone JAR with java -jar 
app.jar. 
Learning 
Curve Requires understanding of Spring configuration before starting. Easier to start with; minimal setup required. 
Goal To provide flexibility and a rich ecosystem for enterprise apps. To simplify Spring development and speed up production 
readiness. 
Example 
Startup 
ApplicationContext context = new 
AnnotationConfigApplicationContext(AppConfig.class); 
SpringApplication.run(App.class, 
args); 
@SpringBootApplication 
=>@EnableAutoConfiguration(It enables AutoConfiguration) 
=>@ComponentScan(Scan for the stereo type annotations in the given package and subpackage) 
=>@Configuration(Marking the class as Configuration class). 
SpringApplication.run() internally uses AnnotationConfigApplicationContext class to create an IOC container by taking java 
class as @Configuration class(in fact it takes current class nothing but ClientApp cum ConfigurationClass) 
Note:  
By default all the components are of Singleton, we can explicitly make it as other scopes using the anotation called 
@Scope(value=" Singleton ") 
Spring SpringBoot 
 It is a framework for JEE 
technologies/Application framework 
 The main feature is DependancyInjection and 
DependancyLookUp. 
 It supports XML driven configuration as a 
inputs to the IOC-Container. 
 Programmer creates IOC container 
explicitly.Allows to devleop spring apps using 
                 XML 
                 XML + Annotation 
                 Pure Java(No XML) 
 Doesn't give embeded server to use in 
webapplications. 
 Doesn't give embeded database/inMemory 
Database 
 It is light weight because no autoconfiguration. 
 No support for "Microservices architecture" 
based application development. 
 It provides abstraction for Spring framework 
and simplifies SpringApp development. 
 The main feature is AutoConfiguration(giving 
common things automatically) 
 Doesn't support XML driven configuration as a 
inputs to the IOC-Container. 
 Programmer doesn't create IOC container 
explicitly it gets created automatically using 
SpringApplication.run(). 
 Supports only one style of configuration that is 
AutoConfiguration where inputs are supplied 
through application.properties/.yml file. 
 It gives embeded server(tomcat server,jetty 
server) to use in web applications. 
 It gives embeded database/InMemory database 
called "H2". 
 It is heavy weight because of 
AutoConfiguration. 
 Support of Microservices architecture is 
extensively avilable. 
First SpringBootProject: 
• The project is a Spring Boot application, as 
indicated by the presence of 
FirstSpringBootProjectApplication.java in the main 
package. 
• It uses Java and follows the standard Maven 
project structure. 
• There is a MessageGenerator component, 
suggesting the project may include functionality 
for generating or handling messages. 
package com.SpringBoot.MessageGenerator; 
import java.time.LocalDateTime; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
@Component(value = "Wmg") 
public class MessageGenerator { 
 @Autowired 
 private LocalDateTime date; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("MessageGenerator.class file is loading..."); 
 } 
 public MessageGenerator() { 
  System.out.println("MessageGenerator Object is Created: Zero Param Constructor..."); 
 }  
 public String getMessage(String User) 
 { 
  int hour =date.getHour(); 
  if (hour >=6 && hour<=12) { 
   return "Hello :: " + User + " Good Morning "; 
  } else if (hour >=12 &&hour <= 16) { 
   return "Hello :: " + User + " Good Afternoon "; 
  } else if (hour >=16 && hour <= 20) { 
   return"Hello :: " + User + " Good Evening "; 
  } else { 
   return "Hello :: " + User + " Good Night "; 
  } 
 } 
} 
package com.SpringBoot;

package com.Cource.Target; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Qualifier; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.Cource.Dependent.IcourceMaterial; 
@Component(value = "student") 
public class Student { 
 static { 
  System.out.println("Student.class file is loading..."); 
 } 
 public Student() { 
  System.out.println("Student Object is Created: Zero Param Constructor..."); 
 } 
 @Autowired 
 @Qualifier(value = "courseId") // This is used to inject the JavaCourceMaterial bean. 
 private IcourceMaterial courseMaterial; 
 public void preparation(String examName) 
 { 
  System.out.println("Preparation started for " + examName + " exam..."); 
  String content = courseMaterial.CourceContent(); 
  double price = courseMaterial.CourcePrice(); 
  System.out.println("preparation is going on with cource content: "+ content+" and cource price: " + price); 
  System.out.println("Preparation completed for " + examName + " exam..."); 
 } 
 public IcourceMaterial getCourseMaterial() { 
  return courseMaterial; 
 } 
 public void setCourseMaterial(IcourceMaterial courseMaterial) { 
  this.courseMaterial = courseMaterial; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "Student [courseMaterial=" + courseMaterial + "]"; 
 }  
}

Customer Interest Project In Spring Boot: 
This project is a Spring Boot JDBC-based CRUD application for Customer 
Management, built using layered architecture: 
 Controller Layer → Handles REST API calls 
 Service Layer → Business logic + DTO ↔ BO conversion 
 DAO Layer → Interacts with Database via JDBC 
 DTO / BO / VO → Patterns to transfer and represent data cleanly 
This structure ensures loose coupling, separation of concerns, and reusability. 
package com.SpringBoot; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.Scanner; 
import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication; 
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication; 
import org.springframework.context.ApplicationContext; 
import com.SpringBoot.Controller.CustomerController; 
import com.SpringBoot.Vo.CustomerVo; 
@SpringBootApplication 
public class SpringBootJdbcProjectApplication { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
 ApplicationContext context  = 
SpringApplication.run(SpringBootJdbcProjectApplication.class, args); 
 CustomerController controller = context.getBean("controller", 
CustomerController.class); 
  CustomerVo vo = InserCustomerData(); 
  String result1 = controller.processResult(vo); 
  System.out.println(result1); 
  int cid = getCustomerInfo(); 
  String result = controller.findById(cid); 
  System.out.println(result); 
  List<CustomerVo> customerList = controller.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
  customerList.forEach(System.out::println); 
 } 
 public static CustomerVo InserCustomerData() { 
  Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Name :: "); 
  String customerName = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Address :: "); 
  String customerAddress = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Amount :: "); 
  String customerAmount = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Time Period :: "); 
  String time = sc.nextLine(); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Rate of Interest :: "); 
  String rate = sc.nextLine(); 
  CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
  vo.setCustomeraddress(customerAddress); 
  vo.setCustomerName(customerName); 
  vo.setPrincipleAmount(customerAmount); 
  vo.setTime(time); 
  vo.setRate(rate); 
  return vo; 
 } 
 public static int getCustomerInfo() { 
  Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
  System.out.print("Enter the Customer Id :: "); 
  int CID = sc.nextInt(); 
  sc.close(); 
  return CID; 
 } 
}

This project is a Spring Boot Hibernate-based CRUD application for Customer Management, built using 
layered architecture: 
 Controller Layer → Handles REST API calls 
 Service Layer → Business logic + DTO ↔ BO conversion 
 DAO Layer → Interacts with Database via JDBC 
 DTO / BO / VO → Patterns to transfer and represent data cleanly 
This structure ensures loose coupling, separation of concerns, and reusability. 
com.Customer 
 Contains the main Spring Boot Application class 
(CustomerHibernateSpringBootApplication.java),which serves 
as the entry point for the project. It initializes the Spring Boot 
context. 
com.Customer.Bo 
 Contains Business Objects (BO). These are plain Java objects 
used to hold business-related logic 
 or data transformations before interacting with DTOs, Entities, 
or Services. 
com.Customer.Controller 
 Contains REST Controllers. For example, 
CustomerController.java handles HTTP requests (GET, 
 POST, PUT, DELETE) related to customer operations. 
CustomerControllerInterface.java defines 
 abstract methods to ensure loose coupling and easier testing. 
com.Customer.Dao 
 Contains Data Access Objects (DAO). These classes handle 
database operations. 
 CustomerDao.java defines methods for CRUD operations, and 
CustomerDAOImpl.java provides 
 actual implementation using Hibernate. 
com.Customer.Dto 
 Contains Data Transfer Objects (DTO). For example, 
CustomerDto.java is used to transfer data 
 between layers (Controller ↔ Service). 
com.Customer.Entity 
 Contains Entity classes mapped to database tables. 
CustomerEntityDtos.java is annotated with 
 JPA/Hibernate annotations (@Entity, @Table, @Id, etc.). 
com.Customer.Service 
 Contains Service layer interfaces and implementations. 
CustomerMgmtService.java defines the 
 service contract, while CustomerMgmtServiceImpl.java 
implements business logic and calls DAO 
 methods. 
com.Customer.Vo 
 Contains Value Objects (VO). CustomerVo.java is used to 
represent data returned to clients (often 
 similar to DTO but focused on API responses). 
com.Hibernate.Utils 
Contains Hibernate utility classes. HibernateUtils.java 
manages SessionFactory and database 
 connections. Hibernate.cfg.xml provides Hibernate 
configuration (DB connection, dialect, entity 
 mapping). 
src/main/resources 
 Holds resource files like application.properties, 
messages, and Hibernate XML configurations. 
src/test/java 
 Contains unit and integration test classes. 
pom.xml 
 Maven configuration file containing dependencies 
(Spring Boot, Hibernate, MySQL, etc.) 
package com.Customer.Vo; 
public class CustomerVo { 
 private String customerName; 
 private String customeraddress; 
 private String principleAmount; 
 private String rate; 
 private String time; 
 private String RateofInterstAmount; 
 public String getRateofInterstAmount() { 
  return RateofInterstAmount; 
 } 
 public void setRateofInterstAmount(String rateofInterstAmount) { 
  RateofInterstAmount = rateofInterstAmount; 
 } 
 public String getCustomerName() { 
  return customerName; 
 } 
 public void setCustomerName(String customerName) { 
  this.customerName = customerName; 
 } 
 public String getCustomeraddress() { 
  return customeraddress; 
 } 
 public void setCustomeraddress(String customeraddress) { 
  this.customeraddress = customeraddress; 
 }

  return principleAmount; 
 }

  return rate;

  this.rate = rate;

  return time;

  this.time = time;

customeraddress=" + customeraddress 
    + ", principleAmount=" + principleAmount + ", rate=" + rate + 
", time=" + time + ", RateofInterstAmount=" + RateofInterstAmount + "]";

package com.Customer.Dao;

public interface CustomerDao {
