package com.Customer.Dao; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.Scanner; 
import javax.sql.DataSource; 
import org.hibernate.HibernateException; 
import org.hibernate.Session; 
import org.hibernate.Transaction; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Repository; 
import com.Customer.Bo.CustomerBo; 
import com.Customer.Entity.CustomeEntityDtos; 
import com.Hibernate.Utils.HibernateUtils; 
@Repository("dao") 
public class CustomerDAOImpl implements CustomerDao { 
 @Autowired 
 private DataSource datasource; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("CustomerDAOImpl class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerDAOImpl(DataSource datasource) { 
  System.out.println("CustomerDAOImpl :: 1 param Constructor..."); 
  this.datasource = datasource; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public int Insert(CustomerBo bo) { 
  Session session = null; 
  org.hibernate.Transaction transaction = null; 
  boolean flag = false; 
  int count = 0; 
  try { 
   session = HibernateUtils.getSession(); 
   if(session != null) { 
    transaction = session.beginTransaction(); 
    CustomeEntityDtos entity = new CustomeEntityDtos(); 
    entity.setCustomer_Name(bo.getCustomerName()); 
    entity.setCustomer_Address(bo.getCustomeraddress()); 
    entity.setPrinciple_Amount(bo.getPrincipleAmount()); 
    entity.setInterestRate(bo.getRate()); 
    entity.setTime(bo.getTime()); 
       session.saveOrUpdate(entity); 
    flag = true; 
    count = 1; // Assuming the insert is successful, set count to 1 
   } 
  } 
  catch(HibernateException e) 
  { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  }catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  finally { 
   if (flag) { 
    transaction.commit(); 
    System.out.println("Transaction Committed Sucessfully...."); 
   } else { 
    transaction.rollback(); 
    System.out.println("Transaction Rolled Back...."); 
   } 
   HibernateUtils.closeSession(); 
  } 
  return count; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public CustomerBo findByID(int id) { 
  Session session = null; 
  CustomerBo customer = null; 
  try { 
   session = HibernateUtils.getSession(); 
   if(session!=null) { 
    CustomeEntityDtos entity = session.get(CustomeEntityDtos.class,id); 
    if(entity !=null) { 
      customer = new CustomerBo(); 
      customer.setCustomerName(entity.getCustomer_Name()); 
      customer.setCustomeraddress(entity.getCustomer_Address()); 
      customer.setPrincipleAmount(entity.getPrinciple_Amount()); 
      customer.setRate(entity.getInterestRate()); 
      customer.setTime(entity.getTime()); 
      System.out.println("Customer Details Fetched 
Sucessfully...."); 
     }  
   } 
  } catch (HibernateException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  finally { 
   HibernateUtils.closeSession(); 
  } 
  return customer; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerBo> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  Session session = null; 
  List<CustomerBo> customerBoList = new ArrayList<CustomerBo>(); 
  try  { 
   session = HibernateUtils.getSession(); 
   if(session!=null) { 
    org.hibernate.query.Query<CustomeEntityDtos> query = 
session.createQuery("FROM  com.Customer.Entity.CustomeEntityDtos", CustomeEntityDtos.class); 
    List<CustomeEntityDtos> entitityList = query.list(); 
    entitityList.forEach( 
      entity->{ 
       CustomerBo customer = new CustomerBo(); 
       customer.setCustomerName(entity.getCustomer_Name()); 
 customer.setCustomeraddress(entity.getCustomer_Address()); 
 customer.setPrincipleAmount(entity.getPrinciple_Amount()); 
       customer.setRate(entity.getInterestRate()); 
       customer.setTime(entity.getTime()); 
       customerBoList.add(customer); 
      } 
              ); 
   } 
  } catch (HibernateException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerBoList; 
 } 
@SuppressWarnings("deprecation") 
 @Override 
 public CustomerBo updateByID(int id) { 
  Session session = null; 
  Transaction transaction = null; 
  CustomerBo bo =null; 
  boolean flag = false; 
  try { 
    session = HibernateUtils.getSession(); 
    if(session != null) { 
     transaction = session.beginTransaction(); 
     CustomeEntityDtos customer = session.get(CustomeEntityDtos.class, id); 
     if(customer!=null) 
     { 
     // System.out.println("Customer Details before Update :: "+customer); 
      bo = new CustomerBo(); 
      Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
      System.out.println("Select the Options to update : 1 for Name, 2 for 
Address, 3 for Principle Amount, 4 for Interest Rate, 5 for Time"); 
      int option = sc.nextInt(); 
      switch (option) { 
       case 1: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Customer Name :: "); 
        String newName = sc.next(); 
        customer.setCustomer_Name(newName); 
        break; 
       case 2: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Customer Address :: "); 
        String newAddress = sc.next(); 
        customer.setCustomer_Address(newAddress); 
        break; 
       case 3: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Principle Amount :: "); 
        float newPrincipleAmount = sc.nextFloat(); 
        customer.setPrinciple_Amount(newPrincipleAmount); 
        break; 
       case 4: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Interest Rate :: "); 
        float newInterestRate = sc.nextFloat(); 
        customer.setInterestRate(newInterestRate); 
        break; 
       case 5: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Time Period :: "); 
        float newTime = sc.nextFloat(); 
        customer.setTime(newTime); 
        break; 
       default: 
        System.out.println("Invalid Option Selected"); 
        System.exit(0); 
      } 
      session.saveOrUpdate(customer); 
      bo.setCustomerName(customer.getCustomer_Name()); 
      bo.setCustomeraddress(customer.getCustomer_Address()); 
      bo.setPrincipleAmount(customer.getPrinciple_Amount()); 
      bo.setRate(customer.getInterestRate()); 
      bo.setTime(customer.getTime()); 
      flag = true; 
      sc.close(); 
     } 
     else { 
      System.out.println("No Customer Found with ID : " + id); 
     } 
    } 
  }catch (HibernateException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } finally { 
   if (flag) { 
    transaction.commit(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Details Updated Successfully...."); 
   } else { 
    transaction.rollback(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Details Update Failed...."); 
   } 
   HibernateUtils.closeSession(); 
  } 
  return bo; 
 } 
@SuppressWarnings("deprecation") 
 @Override 
 public CustomerBo updateByName(String name) { 
  Session session = null; 
  Transaction transaction = null; 
  CustomerBo bo =null; 
  boolean flag = false; 
  try { 
    session = HibernateUtils.getSession(); 
    if(session != null) { 
     transaction = session.beginTransaction(); 
     org.hibernate.query.Query<CustomeEntityDtos> query = session.createQuery("FROM 
com.Customer.Entity.CustomeEntityDtos WHERE Customer_Name = :name", CustomeEntityDtos.class); 
     query.setParameter("name", name); 
     CustomeEntityDtos customer = query.uniqueResult(); 
     if(customer!=null) 
     { 
     // System.out.println("Customer Details before Update :: "+customer); 
      bo = new CustomerBo(); 
      Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); 
      System.out.println("Select the Options to update : 1 for Name, 2 for Address, 3 
for Principle Amount, 4 for Interest Rate, 5 for Time"); 
      int option = sc.nextInt(); 
      switch (option) { 
       case 1: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Customer Name :: "); 
        String newName = sc.next(); 
        customer.setCustomer_Name(newName); 
        break; 
       case 2: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Customer Address :: "); 
        String newAddress = sc.next(); 
        customer.setCustomer_Address(newAddress); 
        break; 
       case 3: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Principle Amount :: "); 
        float newPrincipleAmount = sc.nextFloat(); 
        customer.setPrinciple_Amount(newPrincipleAmount); 
        break; 
       case 4: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Interest Rate :: "); 
        float newInterestRate = sc.nextFloat(); 
        customer.setInterestRate(newInterestRate); 
        break; 
       case 5: 
        System.out.print("Enter the New Time Period :: "); 
        float newTime = sc.nextFloat(); 
        customer.setTime(newTime); 
        break; 
       default: 
        System.out.println("Invalid Option Selected"); 
        System.exit(0); 
      } 
      session.saveOrUpdate(customer); 
      bo.setCustomerName(customer.getCustomer_Name()); 
      bo.setCustomeraddress(customer.getCustomer_Address()); 
      bo.setPrincipleAmount(customer.getPrinciple_Amount()); 
      bo.setRate(customer.getInterestRate()); 
      bo.setTime(customer.getTime()); 
      flag = true; 
      sc.close(); 
     } 
     else { 
      System.out.println("No Customer Found with ID : " + name); 
     } 
    } 
  }catch (HibernateException e) { 
   System.out.println("Multiple Customers Found with Name : " + name+ ". Please use ID to update."); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } finally { 
   if (flag) { 
    transaction.commit(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Details Updated Successfully...."); 
   } else { 
    transaction.rollback(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Details Update Failed...."); 
   } 
   HibernateUtils.closeSession(); 
  } 
  return bo; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public int deleteByID(int id) { 
  Session session = null; 
  Transaction transaction = null; 
  boolean flag = false; 
  int count = 0; 
  try { 
   session = HibernateUtils.getSession(); 
   if(session != null) { 
    transaction = session.beginTransaction(); 
    CustomeEntityDtos customer = session.get(CustomeEntityDtos.class, id); 
    if(customer != null) { 
     session.delete(customer); 
     flag = true; 
     count = 1; // Assuming the delete is successful, set count to 1 
    } else { 
     System.out.println("No Customer Found with ID : " + id); 
    } 
   } 
  } catch (HibernateException e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } finally { 
   if (flag) { 
    transaction.commit(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Deleted Successfully...."); 
   } else { 
    transaction.rollback(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Deletion Failed...."); 
   } 
   HibernateUtils.closeSession(); 
  } 
  return count; 
 }

package com.Customer.Dto;

 } 
 public CustomerDto() 
 { 
  //System.out.println("Customer Object is Created...!");

  return customerName;

  return customeraddress;

  return principleAmount;

  return rate;

  return time;

package com.Customer.Entity; 
import jakarta.persistence.Entity; 
import jakarta.persistence.GeneratedValue; 
import jakarta.persistence.GenerationType; 
import jakarta.persistence.Id; 
import jakarta.persistence.Table; 
@Entity 
@Table(name = "Spring_Customers") 
public class CustomeEntityDtos { 
 @Id 
 @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY) 
 private int CID; 
 private String Customer_Name; 
 private String Customer_Address; 
 private Float Principle_Amount; 
 private Float InterestRate; 
 private Float Time; 
 public CustomeEntityDtos() { 
 // System.out.println("Customer Entity Dtos Object is Created...!"); 
 } 
 public int getCID() { 
  return CID; 
 } 
 public void setCID(int cID) { 
  CID = cID; 
 } 
 public String getCustomer_Name() { 
  return Customer_Name; 
 } 
 public void setCustomer_Name(String customer_Name) { 
  Customer_Name = customer_Name; 
 } 
 public String getCustomer_Address() { 
  return Customer_Address; 
 } 
 public void setCustomer_Address(String customer_Address) { 
  Customer_Address = customer_Address; 
 } 
 public Float getPrinciple_Amount() { 
  return Principle_Amount; 
 } 
 public void setPrinciple_Amount(Float principle_Amount) { 
  Principle_Amount = principle_Amount; 
 } 
 public Float getInterestRate() { 
  return InterestRate; 
 } 
 public void setInterestRate(Float interestRate) { 
  InterestRate = interestRate; 
 } 
 public Float getTime() { 
  return Time; 
 } 
 public void setTime(Float time) { 
  Time = time; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "CustomeEntityDtos [CID=" + CID + ", Customer_Name=" + Customer_Name + ", Customer_Address=" 
    + Customer_Address + ", Principle_Amount=" + Principle_Amount + ", InterestRate=" + 
InterestRate 
    + ", Time=" + Time + "]"; 
 } 
} 
package com.Customer.Service; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.Customer.Dto.CustomerDto; 
public interface CustomerMgmtService { 
    public String CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerDto dto); 
    public String getCustomerInfo(int id); 
    public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
    public CustomerDto updateByID(int id); 
    public CustomerDto updateByName(String name); 
    public int DeleteByID(int id); 
    public String DeleteByName(String name); 
} 
package com.Customer.Service; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service; 
import com.Customer.Bo.CustomerBo; 
import com.Customer.Dao.CustomerDao; 
import com.Customer.Dto.CustomerDto; 
@Service("service") 
public class CustomerMgmtServiceImpl implements CustomerMgmtService { 
 @Autowired 
 private CustomerDao dao; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("CustomerMgmtServiceImpl class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerMgmtServiceImpl(CustomerDao dao) { 
  System.out.println("CustomerMgmtServiceImpl:: 1 Param Constructor....!"); 
  this.dao = dao; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerDto dto) { 
  Float interestAmount = 0.0f; 
  String message = ""; 
  try { 
   interestAmount = (dto.getPrincipleAmount() * dto.getTime() * dto.getRate()) / 
100f; 
   CustomerBo bo = new CustomerBo(); 
   bo.setCustomerName(dto.getCustomerName()); 
   bo.setCustomeraddress(dto.getCustomeraddress()); 
   bo.setPrincipleAmount(dto.getPrincipleAmount()); 
   bo.setRate(dto.getRate()); 
   bo.setTime(dto.getTime()); 
   int count = dao.Insert(bo); 
   if (count == 0) { 
    message = "Customer Regstration is Failed :: " + dto.getPrincipleAmount() 
+ " Interest Amount Rate :: " 
      + interestAmount; 
   } else { 
    message = "Customer Regstration is Sucessfully :: " + 
dto.getPrincipleAmount() 
      + " Interest Amount Rate :: " + interestAmount; 
   } 
   System.out.println("Message :: " + message); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return message; 
 } 
s 
public float CalculateSimpleInterest(CustomerBo bo) { 
  Float interestAmount = 0.0f; 
  String message = ""; 
  try { 
   interestAmount = (bo.getPrincipleAmount() * bo.getTime() * bo.getRate()) / 100f; 
   Float totalAmount = bo.getPrincipleAmount() + interestAmount; 
   if (interestAmount != 0) { 
    message = "Customer Principle Amount :: " + bo.getPrincipleAmount() + " Interest Amount Rate :: 
" 
      + interestAmount + " Total Amount :: " + totalAmount; 
   } else { 
    message = "Customer Does not Exits"; 
   } 
   System.out.println("Message :: " + message); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return interestAmount; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String getCustomerInfo(int id) { 
  String customerInfo = ""; 
  try { 
   CustomerBo customer = dao.findByID(id); 
   if (customer != null) { 
    float intrest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customer); 
    customer.setRateofInterstAmount(intrest); 
    customerInfo = customer.toString(); 
    System.out.println("Customer Info : " + customerInfo); 
   } else { 
    System.out.println("Customer does't Exits....!"); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerInfo; 
 } 
@Override 
 public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerDto> customerDtoList = new ArrayList<CustomerDto>(); 
  try { 
   List<CustomerBo> customerBoList = dao.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
   for (CustomerBo customerBo : customerBoList) { 
    CustomerDto customer = new CustomerDto(); 
    customer.setCustomerName(customerBo.getCustomerName()); 
    customer.setCustomeraddress(customerBo.getCustomeraddress()); 
    customer.setPrincipleAmount(customerBo.getRateofInterstAmount()); 
    customer.setRate(customerBo.getRate()); 
    customer.setTime(customerBo.getTime()); 
    float interest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customerBo); 
    customer.setRateofInterstAmount(interest); 
    customerDtoList.add(customer); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerDtoList; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public CustomerDto updateByID(int id) { 
  CustomerDto customerDto = null; 
  try { 
   System.out.println("CustomerDateils Before Update : " + getCustomerInfo(id)); 
   CustomerBo customerBo = dao.updateByID(id); 
   if (customerBo != null) { 
    customerDto = new CustomerDto(); 
    customerDto.setCustomerName(customerBo.getCustomerName()); 
    customerDto.setCustomeraddress(customerBo.getCustomeraddress()); 
    customerDto.setPrincipleAmount(customerBo.getPrincipleAmount()); 
    customerDto.setRate(customerBo.getRate()); 
    customerDto.setTime(customerBo.getTime()); 
    float interest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customerBo); 
    customerDto.setRateofInterstAmount(interest); 
   } else { 
    System.out.println("No Customer Found with ID : " + id); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerDto; 
 } 
@Override 
 public CustomerDto updateByName(String name) { 
  CustomerDto customerDto = null; 
  try { 
   CustomerBo customerBo = dao.updateByName(name); 
   if (customerBo != null) { 
    customerDto = new CustomerDto(); 
    customerDto.setCustomerName(customerBo.getCustomerName()); 
    customerDto.setCustomeraddress(customerBo.getCustomeraddress()); 
    customerDto.setPrincipleAmount(customerBo.getPrincipleAmount()); 
    customerDto.setRate(customerBo.getRate()); 
    customerDto.setTime(customerBo.getTime()); 
    float interest = CalculateSimpleInterest(customerBo); 
    customerDto.setRateofInterstAmount(interest); 
   } else { 
    System.out.println("No Customer Found with ID : " + name); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerDto; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public int DeleteByID(int id) { 
  try { 
   System.out.println("CustomerDateils Before Delete : " + getCustomerInfo(id)); 
   int count = dao.deleteByID(id); 
   if (count > 0) { 
    System.out.println("Customer Deleted Successfully with ID : " + id); 
   } else { 
    System.out.println("No Customer Found with ID : " + id); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return id; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String DeleteByName(String name) { 
  int count = dao.deleteByName(name); 
  if (count > 0) { 
   return "Customer Deleted Successfully with Name : " + name; 
  } 
  else { 
   return "No Customer Found with Name : " + name; 
  } 
 } 
} 
package com.Customer.Controller; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.Customer.Vo.CustomerVo; 
public interface CustomerControllerInterface { 
 public String findById(int id); 
 public List<CustomerVo> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
 public CustomerVo updateByID(int id); 
 public CustomerVo updateByName(String name); 
 public int DeleteByID(int id); 
 public String DeleteByName(String name); 
} 
package com.Customer.Controller; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.Customer.Dto.CustomerDto; 
import com.Customer.Service.CustomerMgmtService; 
import com.Customer.Vo.CustomerVo; 
@Component("controller") 
public class CustomerController implements CustomerControllerInterface{ 
 @Autowired 
 CustomerMgmtService service; 
 static 
 { 
  System.out.println("CustomerController  class is Loading....."); 
 } 
 public CustomerController(CustomerMgmtService service) 
 { 
  System.out.println("Main Controller:: one param Constructor...!"); 
  this.service = service; 
 } 
 public String processResult(CustomerVo vo) 
 { 
  String Result =""; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   dto.setCustomerName(vo.getCustomerName()); 
   dto.setCustomeraddress(vo.getCustomeraddress()); 
   dto.setPrincipleAmount(Float.parseFloat(vo.getPrincipleAmount())); 
   dto.setRate(Float.parseFloat(vo.getRate())); 
   dto.setTime(Float.parseFloat(vo.getTime())); 
   String result = service.CalculateSimpleInterest(dto); 
   Result = result; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return Result; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String findById(int id) 
 { 
  String result =""; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   result = service.getCustomerInfo(id); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return result; 
 } 
@Override 
 public List<CustomerVo> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerDto> customerDtoList = service.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
  List<CustomerVo> customerVoList = new ArrayList<CustomerVo>(); 
  try { 
   for(CustomerDto customerdto : customerDtoList) 
   { 
    CustomerVo Customervo = new CustomerVo(); 
    Customervo.setCustomerName(customerdto.getCustomerName()); 
 Customervo.setPrincipleAmount(String.valueOf(customerdto.getPrincipleAmount())); 
    Customervo.setRate(String.valueOf(customerdto.getRate())); 
    Customervo.setCustomeraddress(customerdto.getCustomeraddress()); 
    Customervo.setTime(String.valueOf(customerdto.getTime())); 
 Customervo.setRateofInterstAmount(String.valueOf(customerdto.getRateofInterstAmount()))
; 
    customerVoList.add(Customervo); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerVoList; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public CustomerVo updateByID(int id) { 
  // TODO Auto-generated method stub 
  CustomerDto dto = service.updateByID(id); 
  CustomerVo  vo = new CustomerVo(); 
  if(dto!=null) { 
   vo.setCustomerName(dto.getCustomerName()); 
   vo.setCustomeraddress(dto.getCustomeraddress()); 
   vo.setPrincipleAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getPrincipleAmount())); 
   vo.setRate(String.valueOf(dto.getRate())); 
   vo.setTime(String.valueOf(dto.getTime())); 
   vo.setRateofInterstAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getRateofInterstAmount())); 
  } 
  else { 
   System.out.println("No Customer Found with ID : "+id); 
  } 
  return vo; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public CustomerVo updateByName(String name) { 
  // TODO Auto-generated method stub 
  CustomerDto dto = service.updateByName(name); 
  CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
  if(dto!=null) { 
   vo.setCustomerName(dto.getCustomerName()); 
   vo.setCustomeraddress(dto.getCustomeraddress()); 
   vo.setPrincipleAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getPrincipleAmount())); 
   vo.setRate(String.valueOf(dto.getRate())); 
   vo.setTime(String.valueOf(dto.getTime())); 
   vo.setRateofInterstAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getRateofInterstAmount())); 
  } 
  else { 
   System.out.println("No Customer Found with Name : "+name); 
  } 
  return vo; 
 } 
@Override 
 public int DeleteByID(int id) { 
  try { 
   int result = service.DeleteByID(id); 
   if(result > 0) { 
    System.out.println("Customer with ID " + id + " deleted successfully."); 
   } else { 
    System.out.println("No Customer Found with ID : " + id); 
   } 
   return result; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } return id ; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String DeleteByName(String name) { 
  String result = ""; 
  try { 
    result = service.DeleteByName(name); 
   if(result != null) { 
    System.out.println("Customer with Name " + name + " deleted successfully."); 
   } else { 
    System.out.println("No Customer Found with Name : " + name); 
   } 
   return result; 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return result; 
 } 
}

package com.Hibernate.Utils; 
import org.hibernate.HibernateException; 
import org.hibernate.Session; 
import org.hibernate.SessionFactory; 
import org.hibernate.cfg.Configuration; 
public class HibernateUtils { 
 static Configuration config =null; 
 static SessionFactory sessionFactory = null; 
 static Session session = null; 
 static { 
  try { 
    config = new Configuration(); 
    config.configure(); 
    sessionFactory = config.buildSessionFactory(); 
  }catch (HibernateException e) { 
   System.out.println("Hibernate Exception Occured :: "+e.getMessage()); 
  } 
  catch (Exception e) { 
   System.out.println("Exception Occured :: "+e.getMessage()); 
  } 
 } 
 public static Session getSession() { 
  if(session == null || !session.isOpen()) { 
   session = sessionFactory.openSession(); 
   System.out.println("Session is created :: "+session); 
  } 
  return session; 
 } 
 public static void closeSession() { 
  if(session != null && session.isOpen()) { 
   session.close(); 
   System.out.println("Session is closed :: "+session); 
  } 
 } 
 public static void closeSessionFactory() { 
  if(sessionFactory != null && !sessionFactory.isClosed()) { 
   sessionFactory.close(); 
   System.out.println("Session Factory is closed :: "+sessionFactory); 
  } 
 } 
} 
package com.Customer; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.Scanner; 
import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication; 
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication; 
import org.springframework.context.ConfigurableApplicationContext; 
import com.Customer.Controller.CustomerController; 
import com.Customer.Vo.CustomerVo; 
@SpringBootApplication 
public class CustomerHibernateSpringBootApplication { 
    public static void main(String[] args) { 
        ConfigurableApplicationContext appContext = 
                SpringApplication.run(CustomerHibernateSpringBootApplication.class, args); 
        CustomerController controller = appContext.getBean("controller", CustomerController.class); 
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in); // ✅ create only once 
            System.out.println("\n===== Customer Management System ====="); 
            System.out.println("1. Insert Customer"); 
            System.out.println("2. Find Customer by ID"); 
            System.out.println("3. Get All Customers"); 
            System.out.println("4. Update Customer by ID"); 
            System.out.println("5. Update Customer by Name"); 
            System.out.println("6. Delete Customer by ID"); 
            System.out.println("7. Delete Customer by Name"); 
            System.out.println("8. Exit"); 
            System.out.print("Enter your choice: "); 
int choice = sc.nextInt(); 
            sc.nextLine(); // consume leftover newline 
            switch (choice) { 
                case 1: 
                    CustomerVo vo = InserCustomerData(sc); 
                    String result1 = controller.processResult(vo); 
                    System.out.println(result1); 
                    break; 
                case 2: 
                    int cid = enterIdInput(sc); 
                    String result = controller.findById(cid); 
                    System.out.println(result); 
                    break; 
                case 3: 
                    List<CustomerVo> customerList = 
controller.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
                    customerList.forEach(System.out::println); 
                    break; 
                case 4: 
                    int updateId = enterIdInput(sc); 
                    CustomerVo updatedVo = controller.updateByID(updateId); 
                    System.out.println("Updated Customer Details: " + updatedVo); 
                    break; 
                case 5: 
                    String updateName = enterStringInput(sc); 
                    CustomerVo updatedVoByName = controller.updateByName(updateName); 
                    System.out.println("Updated Customer Details: " + 
updatedVoByName); 
                    break; 
                case 6: 
                    int deleteId = enterIdInput(sc); 
                    int deleteResult = controller.DeleteByID(deleteId); 
                    if (deleteResult > 0) { 
                        System.out.println("Customer with ID " + deleteId + " deleted 
successfully."); 
                    } else { 
                        System.out.println("Customer with ID " + deleteId + " not 
found."); 
                    } 
                    break; 
                case 7: 
                    String deleteName = enterStringInput(sc); 
                    String deleteResultByName = controller.DeleteByName(deleteName); 
                    System.out.println(deleteResultByName); 
                    break; 
                case 8: 
                    System.out.println("Thank you for using the Customer Management 
System!"); 
                    break; 
                default: 
                    System.out.println("Invalid choice! Please try again."); 
            } 
        sc.close(); // ✅ close only once at the very end 
    } 
// Method to insert new customer 
    public static CustomerVo InserCustomerData(Scanner sc) { 
        System.out.print("Enter the Customer Name :: "); 
        String customerName = sc.nextLine(); 
        System.out.print("Enter the Customer Address :: "); 
        String customerAddress = sc.nextLine(); 
        System.out.print("Enter the Customer Amount :: "); 
        String customerAmount = sc.nextLine(); 
        System.out.print("Enter the Customer Time Period :: "); 
        String time = sc.nextLine(); 
        System.out.print("Enter the Rate of Interest :: "); 
        String rate = sc.nextLine(); 
        CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
        vo.setCustomeraddress(customerAddress); 
        vo.setCustomerName(customerName); 
        vo.setPrincipleAmount(customerAmount); 
        vo.setTime(time); 
        vo.setRate(rate); 
        return vo; 
    } 
    // Method to read customer id 
    public static int enterIdInput(Scanner sc) { 
        System.out.print("Enter the Customer Id :: "); 
        int cid = sc.nextInt(); 
        sc.nextLine(); // ✅ clear buffer 
        return cid; 
    } 
    // Method to read customer name 
    public static String enterStringInput(Scanner sc) { 
        System.out.print("Enter the Customer Name :: "); 
        return sc.nextLine(); 
    } 
}

There are 2 different ways to perform injection to spring bean properties 
a. @Value => It can be used to inject each value to spring bean properties 
b. @ConfigurationProperties => It can be used to perform bulk injection. 
@Value 
• Purpose: Inject a single value into a bean property. 
• Usage: Can inject values from: 
o application.properties or application.yml 
o System properties 
o Literal values 
@Component 
public class MyBean { 
    @Value("${app.name}") 
    private String appName; 
    @Value("100") 
    private int maxUsers; 
} 
@ConfigurationProperties 
Purpose: Bind a group of related properties (bulk injection) to a Java class. 
Usage: Typically used for structured configuration (like nested properties). 
package com.AppConfig.Company; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Value; 
import org.springframework.boot.context.properties.ConfigurationProperties; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
@Component(value="comp1") 
@ConfigurationProperties(prefix="com.app-config") 
public class Company1 { 
 @Value("${name}") 
 private String name; 
 @Value("${technology}") 
 private String technology; 
 @Value("${location}") 
 private String location; 
 static { 
  System.out.println("Company1.class file is loading..."); 
 } 
 public Company1() { 
  System.out.println("Company1 object is created..."); 
 } 
 public String getName() { 
  return name; 
 } 
 public void setName(String name) { 
  this.name = name; 
 } 
 public String getTechnology() { 
  return technology; 
 } 
 public void setTechnology(String technology) { 
  this.technology = technology; 
 } 
 public String getLocation() { 
  return location; 
 } 
 public void setLocation(String location) { 
  this.location = location; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "Company1 [name=" + name + ", technology=" + technology + ", location=" + location + "]"; 
 } 
}

package com.AppConfig.Company_and_Employee; 
import java.util.Arrays; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.Map; 
import java.util.Set; 
import org.springframework.boot.context.properties.ConfigurationProperties; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
@Component(value = "emp") 
@ConfigurationProperties(prefix = "emp.info") 
public class Employee { 
 private String empName; 
 private long empId; 
 private Company empCompany; 
 private String[] empSkills; 
 private List<String> empProjects; 
 private Set<Long> empMobileNumbers; 
 private Map<String,Object> idDetails; 
 public String getEmpName() { 
  return empName; 
 } 
 public void setEmpName(String empName) { 
  this.empName = empName; 
 } 
 public long getEmpId() { 
  return empId; 
 } 
 public void setEmpId(long empId) { 
  this.empId = empId; 
 }

  return empCompany; 
 }

  this.empCompany = empCompany; 
 } 
 public String[] getEmpSkills() { 
  return empSkills; 
 } 
 public void setEmpSkills(String[] empSkills) { 
  this.empSkills = empSkills; 
 } 
 public List<String> getEmpProjects() { 
  return empProjects; 
 } 
 public void setEmpProjects(List<String> empProjects) { 
  this.empProjects = empProjects; 
 } 
 public Set<Long> getEmpMobileNumbers() { 
  return empMobileNumbers; 
 } 
 public void setEmpMobileNumbers(Set<Long> empMobileNumbers) { 
  this.empMobileNumbers = empMobileNumbers; 
 } 
 public Map<String, Object> getIdDetails() { 
  return idDetails; 
 } 
 public void setIdDetails(Map<String, Object> idDetails) { 
  this.idDetails = idDetails; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "Employee [empName=" + empName + ", empId=" + empId + ", empCompany=" + empCompany 
+ ", empSkills=" 
    + Arrays.toString(empSkills) + ", empProjects=" + empProjects + ", 
empMobileNumbers=" + empMobileNumbers 
    + ", idDetails=" + idDetails + "]"; 
 }

  Employee employee = context.getBean(Employee.class); 
  System.out.println(employee); 
  String[] skills = employee.getEmpSkills(); 
  String empname = employee.getEmpName();

 }

YAML Basics 
YAML → Yet Another Markup Language (.yml / .yaml extension). 
Advantage over .properties → avoids repeated prefixes, supports hierarchical data (collections, HAS-A properties). 
Spring Framework → does not support .yml. 
Spring Boot → supports .yml via snakeyml.jar. 
YAML Writing Rules 
No duplicate nodes/levels. 
Hierarchy → replace . with : and indent (≥1 space). 
Key-value → replace = with : (with space). 
Collections → use - for List/Array/Set. 
Map / HAS-A property → write keys as new nested nodes. 
Comments → use #.

# - The yaml file had comments which are lost in the refactoring!

package com.SprCustomers.Dao; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.SprCustomers.Bo.CustomerBo; 
public interface CustomerDao { 
 public CustomerBo getCustomerDetailsById(int custId); 
 public List<CustomerBo> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Dao; 
import java.sql.Connection; 
import java.sql.PreparedStatement; 
import java.sql.ResultSet; 
import java.sql.SQLException; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import javax.sql.DataSource; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Repository; 
import com.SprCustomers.Bo.CustomerBo; 
@Repository("dao") 
public class CustomerDaoImpl implements CustomerDao { 
 public String selectBYID_Query = "select 
Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time from 
testschema.Spring_Customers where CID = ?"; 
 public String selectAll_Query = "select 
Customer_Name,Customer_Address,Principle_Amount,InterestRate,Time from 
testschema.Spring_Customers"; 
 @Autowired 
 private DataSource datasource; 
 @Override 
 public CustomerBo getCustomerDetailsById(int custId) { 
  CustomerBo customerBo = null; 
  try(Connection connection = datasource.getConnection()){ 
   if(connection!=null) 
   { 
    PreparedStatement preparedStatement = 
connection.prepareStatement(selectBYID_Query); 
    preparedStatement.setInt(1, custId); 
    ResultSet resultSet = preparedStatement.executeQuery(); 
    while(resultSet.next()) { 
     customerBo = new CustomerBo(); 
     customerBo.setCustomerName(resultSet.getString(1)); 
     customerBo.setCustomeraddress(resultSet.getString(2)); 
     customerBo.setPrincipleAmount(resultSet.getFloat(3)); 
     customerBo.setRate(resultSet.getFloat(4)); 
     customerBo.setTime(resultSet.getFloat(5)); 
    } 
   } 
  } catch (SQLException e) { 
   System.out.println("Connection not established"+e.getMessage()); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  }catch (Exception e) { 
   System.out.println("Some other exception"+e.getMessage()); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerBo; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerBo> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  CustomerBo customerBo = null; 
  List<CustomerBo> customerBolist = new ArrayList<CustomerBo>(); 
  try(Connection connection = datasource.getConnection()){ 
   if(connection!=null) 
   { 
    PreparedStatement preparedStatement = 
connection.prepareStatement(selectAll_Query); 
    ResultSet resultSet = preparedStatement.executeQuery(); 
    while(resultSet.next()) { 
     customerBo = new CustomerBo(); 
     customerBo.setCustomerName(resultSet.getString(1)); 
     customerBo.setCustomeraddress(resultSet.getString(2)); 
     customerBo.setPrincipleAmount(resultSet.getFloat(3)); 
     customerBo.setRate(resultSet.getFloat(4)); 
     customerBo.setTime(resultSet.getFloat(5)); 
     //Adding each record to List 
     customerBolist.add(customerBo); 
    } 
   } 
  }  
  catch (SQLException e) { 
   System.out.println("Connection not established"+e.getMessage()); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  catch (Exception e) { 
   System.out.println("Some other exception"+e.getMessage()); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return customerBolist; 
 } 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Service; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerDto; 
public interface CustomerService { 
 public CustomerDto getCustomerDetailsById(int custId); 
 public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
} 
Project Info: 
This project appears to be a Spring-based Java application named 
"YmlSpringJdbcProject." It uses Spring JDBC for database operations and is 
configured using YAML files (application.yml). The provided CustomerDto 
class is a Data Transfer Object representing customer details, including name, 
address, principal amount, rate, time, and interest amount. The project likely 
manages customer data and performs calculations related to interest, 
leveraging Spring's dependency injection and JDBC for persistence. 
package com.SprCustomers.Service; 
import java.util.ArrayList; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service; 
import com.SprCustomers.Bo.CustomerBo; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dao.CustomerDao; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerDto; 
@Service("service") 
public class CustomerServiceImpl implements CustomerService { 
 @Autowired 
 private CustomerDao dao; 
 @Override 
 public CustomerDto getCustomerDetailsById(int custId) { 
  CustomerDto dto = null; 
  try { 
   CustomerBo bo =  dao.getCustomerDetailsById(custId); 
   dto = new CustomerDto(); 
   dto.setCutomerName(bo.getCustomerName()); 
   dto.setCustomerAddress(bo.getCustomeraddress()); 
   dto.setPrincipleAmount(bo.getPrincipleAmount()); 
   dto.setRate(bo.getRate()); 
   dto.setTime(bo.getTime()); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   System.out.println("Exception Occured in Service Layer....!"+e.getMessage()); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return dto; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerDto> listDto = new ArrayList<CustomerDto>(); 
  try { 
   List<CustomerBo> bolist = dao.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
   bolist.forEach(bo-> 
   { 
    CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
    dto.setCutomerName(bo.getCustomerName()); 
    dto.setCustomerAddress(bo.getCustomeraddress()); 
    dto.setPrincipleAmount(bo.getPrincipleAmount()); 
    dto.setRate(bo.getRate()); 
    dto.setTime(bo.getTime()); 
    //Add each dto to listDto 
    listDto.add(dto); 
   }); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   // TODO: handle exception 
  } 
  return listDto; 
 } 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Controller; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.SprCustomers.Vo.CustomerVo; 
public interface CustomerController { 
 public String getCustomerDetailsById(int custId); 
 public List<CustomerVo> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Controller; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.stream.Collectors; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerDto; 
import com.SprCustomers.Service.CustomerService; 
import com.SprCustomers.Vo.CustomerVo; 
@Component("controller") 
public class CustomerControllerImpl implements CustomerController { 
 @Autowired 
 private CustomerService service; 
 @Override 
 public String getCustomerDetailsById(int custId) { 
  String CustomerInfo = null; 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = service.getCustomerDetailsById(custId); 
   CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
   vo.setCname(dto.getCutomerName()); 
   vo.setCaddress(dto.getCustomerAddress()); 
   vo.setPamount(String.valueOf(dto.getPrincipleAmount())); 
   vo.setInterestrate(String.valueOf(dto.getRate())); 
   vo.setTime(String.valueOf(dto.getTime())); 
   CustomerInfo = vo.toString(); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   System.out.println("Exception Occured in Controller 
Layer...!"+e.getMessage()); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return CustomerInfo; 
 } 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerVo> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerVo> listVo = null; 
  try 
  { 
   List<CustomerDto> dtolist = service.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
   listVo = dtolist.stream() 
      .map(dto->{ 
      CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
      vo.setCname(dto.getCutomerName()); 
      vo.setCaddress(dto.getCustomerAddress()); 
      vo.setPamount(String.valueOf(dto.getPrincipleAmount())); 
      vo.setInterestrate(String.valueOf(dto.getRate())); 
      vo.setTime(String.valueOf(dto.getTime())); 
      return vo; 
      }).collect(Collectors.toList()); 
  } 
  catch (Exception e) { 
   System.out.println("Exception Occured in Controller 
Layer...!"+e.getMessage()); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  return listVo; 
 } 
}

package com.SprCustomers; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.Scanner; 
import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication; 
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication; 
import org.springframework.context.ApplicationContext; 
import com.SprCustomers.Controller.CustomerController; 
import com.SprCustomers.Controller.CustomerControllerImpl; 
import com.SprCustomers.Vo.CustomerVo; 
@SpringBootApplication 
public class YmlSpringJdbcProjectApplication { 
 public static void main(String[] args) { 
  ApplicationContext context =SpringApplication.run(YmlSpringJdbcProjectApplication.class, 
args); 
  System.out.println("SpringBoot App Started"); 
  CustomerController controller = context.getBean(CustomerControllerImpl.class); 
  System.out.println("1. Get Customer Details By Id"); 
  System.out.println("2. Get All Customer Details"); 
  System.out.println("3. Exit"); 
  System.out.println("==================================="); 
  System.out.print("Enter Your Choice :: "); 
  try(Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in)){ 
   int choice = sc.nextInt(); 
   switch (choice) { 
   case 1: 
    System.out.print("Enter the Customer Id :: "); 
    int cid = sc.nextInt(); 
    String result = controller.getCustomerDetailsById(cid); 
    System.out.println(result); 
    break; 
   case 2: 
    List<CustomerVo> customerList = controller.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
    customerList.forEach(System.out::println); 
   } 
 }  catch (Exception e) { 
   System.out.println("Exception Occured in Main Method...!"+e.getMessage()); 
   e.printStackTrace(); 
  } 
  System.out.println("==================================="); 
  System.out.println("SpringBoot App Stopped"); 
 } 
}

Project Overview 
The Customer Management System is a full-stack-ready Spring Boot REST API project designed to manage customer financial details 
efficiently. 
It performs complete CRUD (Create, Read, Update, Delete) operations on customer data, including calculation of interest and total 
amount for each customer’s investment details. 
This project demonstrates real-time CRUD implementation using: 
 Spring Boot 
 Spring Data JPA (Hibernate) 
 MySQL Database 
 Lombok 
 Java 8+ Features (Streams, Optional, Lambdas) 
 Postman for API testing 
To build a RESTful backend that allows users to: 
 Insert new customers 
 Retrieve single or all customers 
 Update existing customer details 
 Delete customers by ID 
Each record stores and auto-calculates: 
 Principal Amount 
 Rate of Interest 
 Time (in years) 
 Interest Amount 
 Total Amount 
⚙️ Project Architecture 
com.SprCustomers 
│ 
├── controller        → Handles REST endpoints (CRUD) 
├── service           → Business logic (calculations, validations) 
├── repository        → JPA repository for DB access 
├── dto               → Data Transfer Objects (CustomerDto) 
├── entity (bo)       → JPA entity mapped to MySQL table 
└── application.yml   → Database configuration 
Lombok Library: 
Lombok is a Java library that reduces boilerplate code by auto-generating getters, setters, constructors, toString(), and more 
using simple annotations like @Getter, @Setter, and @Data. It makes classes cleaner, more readable, and easier to maintain, 
especially in Spring Boot projects. 
package com.SprCustomers.Vo; 
import lombok.Getter; 
import lombok.Setter; 
@Getter 
@Setter 
public class CustomerVo { 
 private String customerName; 
 private String customerAddress; 
 private String principalAmount; 
 private String rate; 
 private String time; 
 private String rateofInterstAmount; 
 private String totalAmount; 
 public CustomerVo() {} 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "CustomerVo [customerName=" + customerName + ", customerAddress=" + customerAddress 
    + ", principalAmount=" + principalAmount + ", rate=" + rate + ", time=" + time 
    + ", rateofInterstAmount=" + rateofInterstAmount + ", totalAmount=" + totalAmount + 
"]"; 
 } 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Bo; 
import jakarta.persistence.Column; 
import jakarta.persistence.Entity; 
import jakarta.persistence.GeneratedValue; 
import jakarta.persistence.GenerationType; 
import jakarta.persistence.Id; 
import jakarta.persistence.Table; 
import jakarta.persistence.Transient; 
import lombok.Getter; 
import lombok.Setter; 
@Getter 
@Setter 
@Entity 
@Table(name = "Spring_Customers", schema = "testschema") 
public class CustomerBo { 
 @Id 
 @GeneratedValue(strategy = GenerationType.IDENTITY) 
 @Column(name = "CID") 
 private Integer customerId; 
 @Column(name = "Customer_Name") 
 private String customerName; 
 @Column(name = "Customer_Address") 
 private String customerAddress;  
 @Column(name = "`Interest_Rate`") 
 private Float interestRate; 
 @Column(name = "`Principle_Amount`") 
 private Float principalAmount; 
 @Column(name = "Time") 
 private Float time;   
 @Transient 
 private Float rateofInterstAmount; 
 @Transient 
 private Float totalAmount; 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "CustomerBo [customerId=" + customerId + ", customerName=" + customerName + ", 
customerAddress=" 
    + customerAddress + ", principalAmount=" + principalAmount + ", rate=" + 
interestRate + ", time=" + time 
    + ", rateofInterstAmount=" + rateofInterstAmount + totalAmount + "]"; 
 } 
} 
// @Transient - When you have a field in your entity class that 
you want to use 
 // in 
 // the application logic but not save in the database, 
you mark it with 
 // @Transient 
package com.SprCustomers.Dto; 
import lombok.Getter; 
import lombok.Setter; 
@Setter 
@Getter 
public class CustomerDto { 
 private Integer customerId; 
 private String customerName; 
 private String customerAddress; 
 private Float principalAmount; 
 private Float rate; 
 private Float time; 
 private Float rateofInterstAmount; 
 private Float totalAmount; 
 public CustomerDto() {} 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "CustomerDto [customerId=" + customerId + ", customerName=" + customerName + ", 
customerAddress=" 
    + customerAddress + ", principalAmount=" + principalAmount + ", rate=" + 
rate + ", time=" + time 
    + ", rateofInterstAmount=" + rateofInterstAmount + ", totalAmount=" + 
totalAmount + "]"; 
 } 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Dto; 
import lombok.Getter; 
import lombok.Setter; 
@Setter 
@Getter 
public class CustomerUpdateRequest { 
    private String customerName; 
    private String customerAddress; 
    private Float principalAmount; 
    private Float interestRate; 
    private Float time; 
 @Override 
 public String toString() { 
  return "CustomerUpdateRequest [customerName=" + customerName + ", customerAddress=" + 
customerAddress 
    + ", principalAmount=" + principalAmount + ", interestRate=" + 
interestRate + ", time=" + time + "]"; 
 } 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Dao; 
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.JpaRepository; 
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.Modifying; 
import org.springframework.data.jpa.repository.Query; 
import org.springframework.data.repository.query.Param; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Repository; 
import com.SprCustomers.Bo.CustomerBo; 
import jakarta.transaction.Transactional; 
@Repository 
public interface CustomerRepository extends JpaRepository<CustomerBo, Integer> { 
 @Modifying 
 @Transactional 
 @Query("DELETE FROM CustomerBo c WHERE c.customerId = :id") 
 int deleteByCustomerId(@Param("id") int id); 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Service; 
import java.util.List; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerDto; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerUpdateRequest; 
public interface CustomerService { 
 public CustomerDto getCustomerDetailsById(Integer id); 
 public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
 public int deleteCustomerById(Integer id); 
 public void deleteById(Integer id); 
 public CustomerDto updateCustomerById(Integer id,CustomerUpdateRequest updateRequest); 
 public CustomerDto insertCustomer(CustomerDto customerDto); 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Service; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.Optional; 
import java.util.stream.Collectors; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service; 
import org.springframework.transaction.annotation.Transactional; 
import com.SprCustomers.Bo.CustomerBo; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dao.CustomerRepository; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerDto; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerUpdateRequest; 
@Service 
//@Transactional, which manages database transactions automatically. 
//When you set readOnly = true 
public class customerServiceImpl implements CustomerService { 
 @Autowired 
 private CustomerRepository customerRepository; 
 public customerServiceImpl(CustomerRepository customerRepository) { 
  this.customerRepository = customerRepository; 
 } 
 @Transactional(readOnly = true) 
 @Override 
 public CustomerDto getCustomerDetailsById(Integer id) { 
  return customerRepository.findById(id).map(this::toDto).orElse(null); 
 } 
 @Transactional(readOnly = true) 
 @Override 
 public List<CustomerDto> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  return 
customerRepository.findAll().stream().map(this::toDto).collect(Collectors.toList()); 
 } 
 // DELETE must have write transaction enabled with Custom Method 
 @Transactional 
 @Override 
 public int deleteCustomerById(Integer id) { 
  int count = customerRepository.deleteByCustomerId(id); 
  if (count > 0) { 
   System.out.println("Customer with ID " + id + " deleted successfully....." + 
count); 
   return 1; 
  } 
  return 0; 
 } 
 // DELETE with JPA Repository Method 
 @Override 
 public void deleteById(Integer id) { 
  customerRepository.deleteById(id); 
  System.out.println("Customer with ID " + id + " deleted successfully....."); 
 } 
 // UPDATE - 
 @Override 
 public CustomerDto updateCustomerById(Integer id, CustomerUpdateRequest updateRequest) { 
     Optional<CustomerBo> optionalCustomer = customerRepository.findById(id); 
     if (optionalCustomer.isEmpty()) { 
         return null; 
     } 
     CustomerBo existingCustomer = optionalCustomer.get(); 
     // Update only fields that are not null 
     if (updateRequest.getCustomerName() != null) 
         existingCustomer.setCustomerName(updateRequest.getCustomerName()); 
     if (updateRequest.getCustomerAddress() != null) 
         existingCustomer.setCustomerAddress(updateRequest.getCustomerAddress()); 
     if (updateRequest.getPrincipalAmount() != null) 
         existingCustomer.setPrincipalAmount(updateRequest.getPrincipalAmount()); 
     if (updateRequest.getInterestRate() != null) 
         existingCustomer.setInterestRate(updateRequest.getInterestRate()); 
     if (updateRequest.getTime() != null) 
         existingCustomer.setTime(updateRequest.getTime()); 
     CustomerBo savedCustomer = customerRepository.save(existingCustomer); 
     return toDto(savedCustomer); 
 } 
 @Override 
 public CustomerDto insertCustomer(CustomerDto customerDto) { 
     if (customerDto == null) { 
         throw new IllegalArgumentException("❌ Customer data cannot be null"); 
     } 
     // Convert DTO to Entity 
     CustomerBo bo = new CustomerBo(); 
     bo.setCustomerName(customerDto.getCustomerName()); 
     bo.setCustomerAddress(customerDto.getCustomerAddress()); 
     bo.setPrincipalAmount(customerDto.getPrincipalAmount()); 
     bo.setInterestRate(customerDto.getRate()); 
     bo.setTime(customerDto.getTime()); 
     // Calculate Interest and Total 
     float principal = customerDto.getPrincipalAmount(); 
     float rate = customerDto.getRate(); 
     float time = customerDto.getTime(); 
     float interest = (principal * rate * time) / 100; 
     float total = principal + interest; 
     bo.setRateofInterstAmount(interest); 
     bo.setTotalAmount(total); 
     // Save and Convert Back 
     CustomerBo savedBo = customerRepository.save(bo); 
     return toDto(savedBo); 
 } 
 // Convert Business Object (BO) to Data Transfer Object (DTO) 
 private CustomerDto toDto(CustomerBo bo) { 
  CustomerDto dto = new CustomerDto(); 
  dto.setCustomerId(bo.getCustomerId()); 
  dto.setCustomerName(bo.getCustomerName()); 
  dto.setCustomerAddress(bo.getCustomerAddress()); 
  dto.setPrincipalAmount(bo.getPrincipalAmount()); 
  dto.setRate(bo.getInterestRate()); 
  dto.setTime(bo.getTime()); 
  // Simple Interest = (P * R * T) / 100 
  dto.setRateofInterstAmount((bo.getPrincipalAmount() * bo.getInterestRate() * bo.getTime()) / 100); 
  //total Amount = Principal + Interest 
  dto.setTotalAmount(dto.getPrincipalAmount() + dto.getRateofInterstAmount()); 
  return dto; 
 } 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Controller; 
import java.util.List; 
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerDto; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerUpdateRequest; 
import com.SprCustomers.Vo.CustomerVo; 
public interface CustomerControllerInterface { 
 public ResponseEntity<CustomerVo> getCustomerDetailsById(int id); 
 public ResponseEntity<List<CustomerVo>> getAllCustomerDetails(); 
 public ResponseEntity<String> deleteCustomerById(int id); 
 public ResponseEntity<String> deleteById(int id); 
 public ResponseEntity<String> updateCustomerById(int id,CustomerUpdateRequest updateRequest); 
 public ResponseEntity<String> insertCustomer(CustomerDto customerDto); 
} 
package com.SprCustomers.Controller; 
import java.util.Collections; 
import java.util.List; 
import java.util.stream.Collectors; 
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired; 
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus; 
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity; 
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.DeleteMapping; 
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping; 
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PostMapping; 
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PutMapping; 
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestBody; 
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping; 
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestParam; 
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerDto; 
import com.SprCustomers.Dto.CustomerUpdateRequest; 
import com.SprCustomers.Service.CustomerService; 
import com.SprCustomers.Vo.CustomerVo; 
@RestController 
@RequestMapping("/Spr/customers") 
public class CustomerController implements CustomerControllerInterface { 
 @Autowired 
 private CustomerService service; 
 // ✅ Constructor Injection (Good Practice) 
 public CustomerController(CustomerService service) { 
  this.service = service; 
 } 
 // ================= GET BY ID ==================== 
 @GetMapping("/getCustomerById") 
 public ResponseEntity<CustomerVo> getCustomerDetailsById(@RequestParam int id) { 
  CustomerDto dto = service.getCustomerDetailsById(id); 
  if (dto == null) { 
   return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND).body(null); 
  } 
  CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
  vo.setCustomerName(dto.getCustomerName()); 
  vo.setCustomerAddress(dto.getCustomerAddress()); 
  vo.setPrincipalAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getPrincipalAmount())); 
  vo.setRate(String.valueOf(dto.getRate())); 
  vo.setTime(String.valueOf(dto.getTime())); 
  vo.setRateofInterstAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getRateofInterstAmount())); 
  vo.setTotalAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getTotalAmount())); 
  return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.OK).body(vo); 
 } 
// ================= GET ALL ==================== 
 @GetMapping("/getAllCustomers") 
 public ResponseEntity<List<CustomerVo>> getAllCustomerDetails() { 
  List<CustomerDto> dtolist = service.getAllCustomerDetails(); 
  if (dtolist == null || dtolist.isEmpty()) { 
   return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NO_CONTENT).body(Collections.emptyList()); 
  } 
  List<CustomerVo> listVo = dtolist.stream().map(dto -> { 
   CustomerVo vo = new CustomerVo(); 
   vo.setCustomerName(dto.getCustomerName()); 
   vo.setCustomerAddress(dto.getCustomerAddress()); 
   vo.setPrincipalAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getPrincipalAmount())); 
   vo.setRate(String.valueOf(dto.getRate())); 
   vo.setTime(String.valueOf(dto.getTime())); 
   vo.setRateofInterstAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getRateofInterstAmount())); 
   vo.setTotalAmount(String.valueOf(dto.getTotalAmount())); 
   return vo; 
  }).collect(Collectors.toList()); 
  return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.OK).body(listVo); 
 } 
// ================= DELETE CUSTOM METHOD ==================== 
 @DeleteMapping("/deleteCustomerById") 
 public ResponseEntity<String> deleteCustomerById(@RequestParam int id) { 
     try { 
         // 1️⃣ Fetch details before deletion 
         CustomerDto existingCustomer = service.getCustomerDetailsById(id); 
         if (existingCustomer == null) { 
             return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND) 
                     .body("❌ Customer not found with ID: " + id); 
         } 
         // 2️⃣ Delete the customer 
         service.deleteCustomerById(id); 
         // 3️⃣ Return success message with customer details 
         return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.OK) 
                 .body("✅ Customer Details before Deletion:\n" 
                         + "Customer ID: " + existingCustomer.getCustomerId() + "\n" 
                         + "Name: " + existingCustomer.getCustomerName() + "\n" 
                         + "Address: " + existingCustomer.getCustomerAddress() + "\n" 
                         + "Principal Amount: " + existingCustomer.getPrincipalAmount() + "\n" 
                         + "Rate: " + existingCustomer.getRate() + "\n" 
                         + "Time: " + existingCustomer.getTime() + "\n" 
                         + "Interest Amount: " + existingCustomer.getRateofInterstAmount() + "\n" 
                          +"Total Amount: " + existingCustomer.getTotalAmount() + "\n" 
                         + "Customer Deleted Successfully."); 
     } catch (Exception e) { 
         return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR) 
                 .body("❌ Error while deleting customer: " + e.getMessage()); 
     } 
 } 
 @Override 
 // ================= DELETE BY USING SPING JPA METHOD==================== 
  @DeleteMapping("/deleteCID") 
 public ResponseEntity<String> deleteById(int id) { 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = service.getCustomerDetailsById(id); 
   if(dto==null) 
   { 
    return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND).body("Customer with ID " + id + " not 
found."); 
   } 
   else 
   { 
    service.deleteById(id); 
    return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.OK) 
      .body("✅ Customer Details before Deletion:\n" 
                          + "Customer ID: " + dto.getCustomerId() + "\n" 
                          + "Name: " + dto.getCustomerName() + "\n" 
                          + "Address: " + dto.getCustomerAddress() + "\n" 
                          + "Principal Amount: " + dto.getPrincipalAmount() + "\n" 
                          + "Rate: " + dto.getRate() + "\n" 
                          + "Time: " + dto.getTime() + "\n" 
                          + "Interest Amount: " + dto.getRateofInterstAmount() + "\n" 
                          +"Total Amount: " + dto.getTotalAmount() + "\n" 
                          + "Customer Deleted Successfully."); 
   } 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
    return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR) 
                  .body("❌ Error while deleting customer: " + e.getMessage()); 
  }  
 } 
 @PutMapping("/updateCustomerById") 
 public ResponseEntity<String> updateCustomerById(@RequestParam int id, 
                                                  @RequestBody CustomerUpdateRequest updateRequest) { 
     try { 
         CustomerDto updatedCustomer = service.updateCustomerById(id, updateRequest); 
         if (updatedCustomer == null) { 
             return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND) 
                     .body("❌ Customer with ID " + id + " not found."); 
         } 
         String response = String.format(""" 
                 ✅ Customer Updated Successfully: 
                 -------------------------------- 
                 ID: %d 
                 Name: %s 
                 Address: %s 
                 Principal Amount: %.2f 
                 Interest Rate: %.2f 
                 Time: %.2f 
                 Interest Amount: %.2f 
                 Total Amount: %.2f 
                 """, 
                 updatedCustomer.getCustomerId(), 
                 updatedCustomer.getCustomerName(), 
                 updatedCustomer.getCustomerAddress(), 
                 updatedCustomer.getPrincipalAmount(), 
                 updatedCustomer.getRate(), 
                 updatedCustomer.getTime(), 
                 updatedCustomer.getRateofInterstAmount(), 
                 updatedCustomer.getTotalAmount(), 
                 updatedCustomer.getTotalAmount() 
         ); 
         return ResponseEntity.ok(response); 
     } catch (Exception e) { 
         return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR) 
                 .body("❌ Error while updating customer: " + e.getMessage()); 
     } 
 } 
 @PostMapping("/insertCustomer") 
 @Override 
 public ResponseEntity<String> insertCustomer(@RequestBody CustomerDto customerDto) { 
  try { 
   CustomerDto dto = service.insertCustomer(customerDto); 
   if (dto == null) { 
    return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST).body("❌ Invalid customer data 
provided."); 
   } 
   String response = String.format(""" 
     ✅ Customer Inserted Successfully: 
     -------------------------------- 
     ID: %d 
     Name: %s 
     Address: %s 
     Principal Amount: %.2f 
     Interest Rate: %.2f 
     Time: %.2f 
     Interest Amount: %.2f 
     Total Amount: %.2f 
     """, 
     dto.getCustomerId(), 
     dto.getCustomerName(), 
     dto.getCustomerAddress(), 
     dto.getPrincipalAmount(), 
     dto.getRate(), 
     dto.getTime(), 
     dto.getRateofInterstAmount(), 
     dto.getTotalAmount() 
   ); 
   return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CREATED).body(response); 
  }catch (IllegalArgumentException e) { 
   return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST).body("❌ " + e.getMessage()); 
  } catch (Exception e) { 
   return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR) 
     .body("❌ Error while inserting customer: " + e.getMessage()); 
  } 
 } 
}

BUILD PROCESS: 
* What is Build Process? 
The build process involves preparing, compiling, testing, and packaging software for deployment. 
Steps: 
1. Develop Java source code & resources 
2. Organize files into folders 
3. Add required JARs/libraries to classpath 
4. Compile source code 
5. Execute & test code (Unit Testing) 
6. Package the app (JAR/WAR) for release 
⚙️ Problems with Manual Build 
 - Repetitive & time-consuming 
 - Mistakes in order or missing steps 
 - Hard to manage large projects 
�
� Batch File Automation (.bat) 
Automates build steps using command scripts. 
Limitations: 
 - No conditional logic or dependencies 
 - No dynamic JAR download 
 - Not self-configuring (declarative) 
�
� Ant Tool 
 Improved automation with XML and dependencies. 
 Limitations: Still manual and complex. 
�
� Maven - Project Management Tool 
Maven automates build, dependency management, testing, and packaging. 
�
� Apache Maven is a build automation and project management tool used mainly for Java projects. 
It helps developers compile, test, package, and manage project dependencies easily and automatically. 
Key Features: 
1. Default project structures (archetypes) 
2. Auto-downloads dependencies 
3. Supports multiple repositories 
4. Generates JAR/WAR/EAR files 
5. Runs tests & reports 
6. Manages multi-module projects 
7. Generates documentation 
8. Uses plugins for extra functionality 
�
�️ Maven Archetypes: 
 - maven-archetype-quickstart → For standalone Java projects 
 - maven-archetype-webapp → For web applications 
�
�️ Installing Maven: 
1. Download Maven ZIP from https://maven.apache.org/download.cgi 
2. Set environment variables: 
   - PATH = <MAVEN_HOME>\bin 
   - JAVA_HOME = <JDK_PATH> 
3. Verify: mvn –version 
�
� Maven Repositories: 
Types: 
1. Central Repository → Online (Apache) 
2. Local Repository → User machine (.m2 folder) 
3. Remote Repository → Third-party companies 
Each item identified by GAV: - GroupId → Organization name - ArtifactId → Project/module name - Version → Library version 
�
� Creating Maven Project (CLI) 
Command: 
mvn archetype:generate 
Inputs: - groupId, artifactId, version, package 
Structure: 
MathProj1/ 
 ├── src/main/java 
 ├── src/test/java 
 ├── pom.xml 
 └── target/ 
⚡ Common Maven Commands ----------------------------------- 
mvn compile         → Compile source code 
mvn test            → Run unit tests 
mvn package         → Package JAR/WAR 
mvn clean           → Delete target folder 
mvn clean package   → Clean + build 
 ----------------------------------- 
�
� JUnit Testing ----------------------------------- 
Tests in src/test/java (e.g., AppTest.java) 
Commands: - mvn test - mvn surefire-report:report (HTML report) - mvn site (Documentation report) 
MAVEN LIFECYCLE COMMANDS 
Maven has 3 lifecycles: 
1. clean (3 phases) 
2. default (23 phases) 
3. site (4 phases) 
Maven Lifecycle Commands: 
mvn validate      → Validate project structure and dependencies 
mvn compile       → Compile source code 
mvn test          → Run unit tests 
mvn package       → Package compiled code into JAR/WAR 
mvn verify        → Verify project meets quality criteria 
mvn install       → Install JAR/WAR into local repository 
mvn deploy        → Deploy build to remote repository 
mvn site          → Generate project documentation 
mvn clean         → Remove previous builds 
mvn clean install → Clean and install in local repository 
mvn dependency:tree → Show dependency hierarchy 
 --------------------------- 
| Tool     | Description | 
|----------|--------------| 
| Batch    | Automates commands, no logic or dependencies | 
| Ant      | XML-based build tool, supports dependencies | 
| Maven    | Full project management tool (build, test, package, report, dependency management) | 
✅ Maven Life Cycles 
1. clean → Deletes old builds 
2. default → Compiles, tests, packages 
3. site → Generates reports & documentation 
Invasive vs Non-Invasive Programming ------------------------------------ - Invasive: When your code is tightly coupled with the framework. 
  - Example: A SpringBean class with proprietary annotations like @Component, @Autowired, 
@Qualifier. - Non-Invasive: When your code is loosely coupled and can work without the framework (or with less 
dependency). 
  - Example: Using standard Java Config Annotations (JSR-330) like @Named, @Inject, @Resource. 
  - Note: Pure non-invasive programming is difficult in complex apps, so a mix is often favored: 
    a. Java Config Annotation (First choice) 
    b. Spring Annotations 
    c. Third-party Annotations 
    d. Custom Annotations 
Java Config Annotation (JSR-330) -------------------------------- - Requires "javax.inject" dependency. - @Inject: Can be used at field, constructor, or setter level. - @Named: Used to name a bean or resolve ambiguity (similar to @Qualifier). - @Resource: Can be used at field or setter level (but not constructor). Requires "name" parameter for 
ambiguity resolution. 
Purpose:  
To demonstrate Dependency Injection using standard Java Config annotations (@Inject, 
@Named) instead of Spring-specific annotations (@Autowired, @Component), and how 
to integrate legacy XML configuration with Java Configuration. 
Flow: 
1. Main Class: BootProj07DependencyInjectionJavaConfigurationApplication - Annotated with @SpringBootApplication. - Uses @ImportResource to load "in/ineuron/cfg/applicationContext.xml". - Bootstraps the application and retrieves the Student bean. - Calls methods on the Student object to demonstrate DI. 
2. Beans: - Student (@Named("std")): The target bean. It injects a course material. - ICourseMaterial (Interface): Defines contract for course materials. - JavaCourseMaterial (@Named("java")): Implementation for Java. - DotNetCourseMaterial (@Named("dotNet")): Implementation for .NET. 
3. Configuration: - "application.properties" defines "course.choose=java". - "applicationContext.xml" uses this property to alias @Named("java") to "courseId". - Student injects @Named("courseId"), which resolves to the Java implementation 
dynamically. 
Real Scenario: 
This approach is useful when migrating legacy Spring applications (XML-based) to 
Spring Boot, or when using JSR-330 standard annotations (javax.inject) to keep code 
loosely coupled from the Spring Framework (Non-Invasive). 
Configuring an Object in Xml file: 
<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?> 
<beans xmlns="http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans" 
xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" 
xsi:schemaLocation="http://www.springframework.org/schema/beans 
https://www.springframework.org/schema/beans/spring-beans.xsd"> 
<alias name="${course.choose}" alias="courseId" /> 
</beans> 
Application.properties: 
course.choose=java 
package in.ineuron.comp; 
import javax.inject.Inject; 
import javax.inject.Named; 
import in.ineuron.dependent.ICourseMaterial; 
@Named("std") 
public class Student { 
    static { 
        System.out.println("Student.class file is loading..."); 
    } 
    public Student() { 
        System.out.println("Student Object is instantiated..."); 
    } 
    @Inject 
    @Named(value="courseId") 
    private ICourseMaterial material; 
    public void preparation(String examName) { 
        System.out.println("Preparation started for :: " + examName); 
        String courseContent = material.courseContent(); 
        double price = material.price(); 
        System.out.println("Prepartion is going on using :: " + courseContent + " material 
with price :: " + price); 
        System.out.println("Preparation completed for :: " + examName); 
    } 
    public ICourseMaterial getMaterial() { 
        return material; 
    } 
    public void setMaterial(ICourseMaterial material) { 
        this.material = material; 
    } 
    @Override 
    public String toString() { 
        return "Student [material=" + material + "]"; 
    } 
} 
package in.ineuron; 
import java.util.Arrays; 
import org.springframework.boot.SpringApplication; 
import org.springframework.boot.autoconfigure.SpringBootApplication; 
import org.springframework.context.ApplicationContext; 
import org.springframework.context.ConfigurableApplicationContext; 
import org.springframework.context.annotation.ImportResource; 
import in.ineuron.comp.Student; 
@SpringBootApplication 
@ImportResource(locations = "in/ineuron/cfg/applicationContext.xml") 
public class BootProj07DependencyInjectionJavaConfigurationApplication { 
    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception { 
        ApplicationContext context = SpringApplication 
                .run(BootProj07DependencyInjectionJavaConfigurationApplication.class, args); 
        System.out.println("Beans info are :: " + Arrays.toString(context.getBeanDefinitionNames())); 
        System.out.println(); 
        Student student = context.getBean(Student.class); 
        System.out.println(student); 
        student.preparation(student.getMaterial().getClass().getName()); 
        ((ConfigurableApplicationContext) context).close(); 
    } 
}
